The Beining Railway Bonds Will Be Issued in Advance

Nanjing, The Beining Railway Bureau plans to issue 5 million yuan of short-term railway locomotive equipment bonds, which were originally scheduled to be issued in two batches. The first batch, totaling 1.8 million yuan, was scheduled to be issued in November of this year and January of the 20th year. The second batch of 3.2 million yuan was originally planned to be issued after the first batch of bonds was paid off. Now, it is heard that the bureau's passenger and freight traffic is gradually increasing sharply, and the 20 locomotives purchased in the first batch are still not enough to meet the demand. Therefore, the second batch of vehicles should also be scheduled for bidding as soon as possible. It is now planned to issue the second batch of bonds in advance in July of next year. The regulations have been amended and submitted by the Ministry of Railways to the government and Yuan for submission to the Legislative Yuan for review. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

International News

The German Government Decides to Maintain the Status Quo

The Question of Whether to Stay or Leave Will Be Determined After the New Parliament is Convened

Planning to Form a Mixed Cabinet of Moderate Factions

Reuters, Berlin, 15th: German Chancellor Dr. Brüning is said to have received President Hindenburg's permission for the current government to remain in office temporarily until the new parliament convenes on October 14th. Negotiations are currently underway to form a mixed cabinet of moderate factions, which may include the Social Democrats, but excluding the Nazi Party and the Communist Party. Nazi leader Hitler announced his policy platform on the eve of the election, advocating (1) the abolition of the policy of begging France for favors, (2) the establishment of a strong German army, and (3) the rejection of the Young Plan. The Nazi Party's victory is largely attributed to the announcement of this policy.

Kokumin News Agency, Berlin, 16th: This morning, the cabinet convened to discuss measures to deal with the temporary political situation. It was immediately decided that, in accordance with the current constitution, the government must temporarily maintain its status quo and prepare to submit to the new parliament, which will convene on October 13th, a special financial plan formulated by the president based on Article 48 of the constitution after the dissolution of the previous parliament. At the same time, the Brüning cabinet is making every effort to seek the cooperation of the Social Democratic Party to consolidate its position. Although it is not easy to achieve this, given that both sides are unwilling to allow political ruptures to occur again and are deeply concerned about political and economic stability, they will ultimately cooperate. According to outside reports, some people are negotiating to unite the small parties in the new parliament, such as the farmers, conservatives, and civil rights groups, and promote Sir Westarp as their leader to seize a portion of the power. This new group will be composed of representatives from forty parties. Its strength will be no less than that of the right-wing civil rights party led by Hugenberg.

Kokumin News Agency, Berlin, 15th: According to the latest official report, the new German parliament will have 576 members, the most of any parliament since the end of the European War. This is because Germany uses a system of proportional representation, where the number of members of parliament is proportional to the number of votes cast, with approximately one member of parliament being produced for every 60,000 votes. Therefore, the number of members of parliament varies from session to session. The approximate number of seats for each party this time is as follows: Social Democratic Party 143 (152 in the previous session), National Socialist Party 107 (12 in the previous session), Communist Party 76 (54 in the previous session), Catholic Center Party 68 (61 in the previous session), National Right Party 41 (79 in the previous session), National People's Party 30 (45 in the previous session), Economic Party 23 (same in the previous session), State Party 20 (25 in the previous session), Bavarian National Party 19 (17 in the previous session), and other small parties totaling 49. The new parliament is scheduled to convene on October 13th, the latest date stipulated in the constitution. Because the seats in the parliament hall are insufficient, it is necessary to remove a portion of the gallery and renovate it, which takes time, so the convening had to be postponed. According to the regulations, the German parliament building was originally designed to accommodate 400 seats. After the war, the number of members of parliament gradually increased with the adoption of proportional representation, resulting in a situation where it could not accommodate them. This is also different from the situation in other countries. At present, those who talk about politics naturally focus on the sharp increase in the number of votes for extreme progressives. However, most newspapers solemnly declare that the majority of Germans firmly advocate a policy of peace and goodwill in international affairs and will not allow radical ideas to overthrow the parliamentary system domestically. Therefore, the general opinion is that Chancellor Brüning will immediately try to concentrate the strength of the moderate factions and first seek cooperation with the Social Democratic Party to form a large mixed cabinet. The party's official newspaper (Vorwärts) has also expressed a willingness to resolve disputes and make peace, declaring in its commentary that the time has come for the republican parties to abandon their old grudges and work together to cope with the crisis. The Deutsche Tageszeitung also stated that no matter which party the future cabinet belongs to, it will not lightly make foolish trials and tribulations. Even if the National Socialist Party holds power, it will not dare to take huge risks in diplomacy and endanger past victories. The German nation and the state have a clear understanding. Even if the election results show temporary fanaticism, they will soon calm down and return to their original state. This is the argument of the official newspapers of the left and right wings of the moderate faction, which can be regarded as a representation of the general psychology of the German people, except for extremists, and is sufficient to show that the rumors in other countries about the formation of a joint cabinet of the Communist and National Socialist parties that would endanger foreign policy are not based on a deep understanding of the basic beliefs of the German people.

Kokumin News Agency, Geneva, 15th: All sectors of the League of Nations were surprised by the results of the German election. France was initially very fearful of the rise of the National Socialist Party, but was somewhat relieved by the complete failure of the Conservative Party led by Dr. Treviranus. When a news reporter inquired about the German election with French Foreign Minister Briand, Briand said that he was not in a position to express his opinion, as he feared being seen as interfering in German domestic affairs. However, in terms of German foreign policy, he believed that although the composition of parliament had changed, it would remain the same as before.

Pacific News Agency, Paris, 15th: The Paris newspapers commented on the German election results with great enthusiasm. The evening papers published editorials discussing the impact of the victory of the extreme parties. The victory of the Nazi Party led by Hitler was unexpected and considered strange. The position of Chancellor Brüning was generally considered unstable. If the central parties could reunite, he might be able to remain in office. In short, the victory of the extreme parties will have a great impact on the matters under discussion in Geneva. The Discussion newspaper stated that this election result is not to be feared, as European public opinion, although it has changed, is still fond of peace. The Times stated that Germany will know when it is in a difficult position. A new element has emerged in Berlin politics, and European politicians cannot forget it. As for Germany not being allowed to make mistakes again, the same is true for Europe.

Records of the League of Nations Parliament

German Foreign Minister Delivers Important Speech

Kokumin News Agency, Geneva, 15th: The chairman of the League of Nations Parliament announced that there were still fourteen people scheduled to speak on the agenda. In addition to the usual morning session on Tuesday, the general assembly would continue in the afternoon and evening. This was unprecedented in the history of the League of Nations. The French side indicated that Briand had been persuaded by British Foreign Secretary Henderson to agree to submit the European Federal Plan to the Sixth Committee for review. The two had drafted a motion to this effect, which would be submitted to the general assembly tomorrow. All twenty-seven European countries would attend the committee and have the right to vote. When the general assembly continued this morning, Yugoslav Foreign Minister Marinkovic spoke, advocating that the European Federal Plan be discussed by a separate specialized committee, opposing the motion submitted by Swiss representative Motta to refer it to the original general committee. Afterwards, Japanese representative Matsunaga spoke, strongly stating that the Japanese government attaches importance to the issue of disarmament and hopes that the London Naval Treaty will be a precursor to a global naval reduction convention. As for the European Federal Plan, Japan has sympathy for this movement and fully believes that its future realization will not harm the interests of countries outside Europe. At the afternoon session, Hungarian representative Count Apponyi first spoke, welcoming the concept of a European Federation, but strongly advocating that economic issues should take precedence and that the cooperation of the United States was necessary to resolve such issues. He then discussed the peace treaty, stating that the day when this matter would be submitted for discussion based on the principles of fairness and equality was not far off. He also stated that war was ultimately not a tool for resolving such issues. At this point, the audience applauded thunderously. Next, Italian representative Michelis spoke, stating that the global agricultural predicament was the root cause of the current industrial decline, so industry could not be revitalized without restoring agriculture. Finally, representatives from two South American countries spoke, stating that the pursuit of world peace should not be limited to Europe alone. It was reported that the Franco-Italian naval preparatory talks had made satisfactory progress due to the mediation of British Foreign Secretary Henderson. It was expected that Italian Foreign Minister Grandi would arrive here from Rome on Wednesday or Thursday to hold direct talks with French Foreign Minister Briand. This evening, British Minister of Trade Graham hosted a press conference, expressing his support for the movement jointly initiated by the Scandinavian countries and the Netherlands to establish an international committee to define the meaning of the most-favored-nation clause in the treaties of various countries. He also stated that Britain opposes any preferential tariff system. He then discussed British imperial trade and the future imperial conference. Graham reiterated this statement, but declined to discuss any specific issues within it.

Reuters, Geneva, 15th: Italian representative De Michelis stated at the League of Nations conference today that Italy is now willing to ratify the tariff truce convention, which stipulates the continuation of existing trade agreements for one year, with the condition that tariff rates cannot be increased during this period unless absolutely necessary. If an increase is necessary, other countries must be given the opportunity to negotiate before it is implemented. According to a statement made by British Trade Minister Graham at the League of Nations Parliament on the 13th of this month, Britain will ratify this agreement on November 1st of this year and requested that other countries also ratify it at that time so that the signatory countries can meet to determine whether the agreement has been ratified by a majority of countries. It would be regrettable if the number of ratifications was insufficient at that time and the agreement could not be implemented.

Reuters, Geneva, 16th: At today's League of Nations Parliament meeting to discuss the general work of the League of Nations, German Foreign Minister Curtius delivered a speech that was heard by all, stating that the League of Nations is an element of German policy and that Germany intends to support the League of Nations with all its strength. He also stated that countries should not harbor the possibility of war in their minds. Today, we not only have the necessity to avoid war, but we must also eliminate the disputes that cause war. The listeners cheered for him.

Kokumin News Agency, Geneva, 16th: When Foreign Minister Curtius attended and spoke at the League of Nations for the first time this morning, the audience cheered enthusiastically, expressing their warm welcome. This proves that the recent rumors in newspapers that the German election had greatly damaged Curtius' prestige at the Geneva Conference were completely untrue. Curtius stated that since Germany joined the League of Nations, although there have been many disappointments, Germany still attaches great importance to the League of Nations. The first goal of our coming here is to permanently eliminate war, but there are many ways to eliminate war. It is better to prevent it than to contain it, as the method of containment is prone to going astray. Therefore, we strongly support the establishment of a judicial committee to specialize in examining the issue of peace guarantees. Curtius then discussed the issue of reducing armaments, stating that although there have been many discussions on this matter, no actual progress has been made. He said that he was very satisfied with the remarks of British Foreign Secretary Henderson. The disarmament conference should be held next year no matter what, and at that time, measures should be taken to reduce armaments at all costs. Curtius then discussed the case of protecting small and weak nations, stating that the League of Nations should not stand idly by, but should strive to improve their current situation. This is why he advocated that this case should be examined by the League of Nations Sixth Political Committee. This issue is not only related to one country or one nation, but its impact is widespread throughout the world. As for the European Federal Plan promoted by French Foreign Minister Briand, Curtius' opinion was that he admired Briand's ambition in expanding this minority of private claims into a formal motion for the general public to consider. Of all countries, Germany is the most concerned about international understanding, because it is located in the center of Europe. Unfortunately, although Germany has strived for international understanding in recent years, it has not been able to achieve complete harmony. In Curtius' view, the European Federal Plan is best considered by a specially formed committee, but this committee should include all European countries, regardless of whether they are members of the League of Nations or not, and regardless of their political and economic organization, they should be allowed to join.

Japanese Political Situation Remains Grim

The Privy Council and the Government Hold Conflicting Attitudes

The Fate of the London Treaty Will Be Decided at the Imperial Conference

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th: Yesterday, the Privy Council's scrutiny committee and the government clashed head-on, causing great tension in all aspects of the political world last night. The Privy Council side declared that major treaties involving national defense limits cannot be taken lightly and adopted a tougher stance. Privy Council Chairman Kuraoka summoned Vice Chairman Hiranuma and two chief secretaries to his private residence in Akasaka Tanocho at 9:15 this morning to discuss countermeasures. Privy Council advisor Eki Chizuru also visited Ito, chairman of the scrutiny committee, at his private residence in Nagatacho at 9:40 this morning to hear about the committee's progress and express his personal opinions before resigning at 11:00. Eki's visit was the same as General Fukuda's, in that he took the initiative to try to break the impasse. However, some rumors claimed that Ito, in preparation for a split with the government at the Imperial Conference, first sought the understanding of advisors Fukuda and Eki, and then needed to seek the understanding of advisors Okada and Ishii. On the government side, a regular cabinet meeting was held at 10:00 this morning. Prime Minister Hamaguchi gave a detailed report on the progress of the scrutiny committee. After discussion, it was unanimously decided that the government should proceed in accordance with its established policy in order to have the treaty ratified. It was also decided that Prime Minister Hamaguchi would be entrusted with all measures to deal with the Privy Council and all other matters. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 p.m. At present, the political situation has not yet seen a glimmer of hope, and the future remains bleak.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th: The fate of the London Treaty will be decided at the Imperial Conference. Among the advisors to the Privy Council's plenary session, besides the committee members, there are also considerable supporters of the treaty. If all the cabinet members join these advisors, the government side can obtain a majority of three to reject the scrutiny committee's review. At this time, newly appointed scrutiny committee members will be added.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th: Regarding the suspension of the scrutiny by the Privy Council committee, the government observed that, in terms of legal interpretation, the Privy Council cannot simply rely on the committee's report to answer with a "cannot review" response. It is also customary for the committee to reach a unanimous agreement. The committee must first persuade both Mizumachi and Ta. Moreover, it is even more difficult to reach a consensus on the "cannot review" opinion at the Privy Council's formal meeting. A review of the 23 advisors from various factions at the formal meeting, excluding Marquis Kuki Ryuichi, Viscount Ishiguro Tadanori, and Ishihara Kenzo, who were absent due to illness, and Chamberlain Suzuki, who was absent to avoid suspicion, reveals that those who support the treaty among the remaining advisors include Kesaroku Mizumachi, Ryohei Okada, Kikujiro Ishii, Eki Chizuru, Yataro Fukuda, and Kenjiro Tagawa. In addition, Masaakira Tomii, Teiji Sakurai, Kowi Furuichi, and Itaru Matsumuro may not be willing to support the "cannot review" resolution. If a majority vote is contested, the government has 13 ministers and 4 supporting advisors, already obtaining a majority and ensuring a government victory. If the "cannot review" resolution is rejected at the Privy Council's formal meeting, Chairman Kuraoka of the Privy Council, Chairman Ito of the committee, and the other committee members will not be able to remain in their positions with composure due to public perception. Therefore, Chairman Kuraoka and Chairman Ito will carefully consider the committee's decision before the committee meeting is held on the 17th, and

Page 8

first reach a compromise plan to try to break the impasse.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th: The leaders of the Constitutional Democratic Party met at the Marunouchi Industrial Club today to discuss the Privy Council issue and related financial and political issues. They all agreed that the government is not in an unfavorable position in the current situation and decided to fully trust Prime Minister Hamaguchi to monitor the development of the situation. The younger generation of the party's antipathy towards the Privy Council remains strong, and there is a tendency to impeach the Privy Council.

London to Hold a Large Car Exhibition

Reuters, London, 15th: The world's largest car exhibition will be held in London next month. British car manufacturers are now actively promoting their cars on display in order to occupy a larger position in the global car market. Seventy-four car manufacturers are participating in the exhibition, the most from Britain, followed by the United States, and then France, Italy, Germany, and Belgium. It is reported that they will all lower prices to attract customers. The cheapest British-made cars will be sold for £125, and the most expensive for £3,000. Several British manufacturers will display six-cylinder cars with prices the same as or cheaper than similar American-made cars.

Reuters, London, 16th: Mr. Massieux departed from the Croydon Aerodrome at dawn today in a Moth aircraft with 120 horsepower, flying to Australia, hoping to break the record for flying to Australia alone. He plans to travel via Sofia, Bandar Abbas, Calcutta, Bangkok, Darwin, and other places.

Reuters, London, 15th: Five British aviators will compete in a friendly race of 10,000 miles from England to Australia, hoping to break the record of 15 and a half days set by Hinkler in 1928. The first to depart tomorrow will be Mr. Massieux, a teacher at the London Aviation Club, who is also the flight instructor of Ms. Amy Johnson.

In the current situation, it is impossible to increase taxes, and the increase in expenditures continues unabated. Therefore, it is necessary to strictly economize. 87th Meeting of the Executive Yuan

The Executive Yuan held its 87th meeting on the 16th. Those present were Tan Yankai, Sun Ke, Yi Peiji, Wang Boqun, Wang Zhengting, and Liu Ruiheng. Those in attendance were Chen Shaokuan, Zheng Hongnian, Liu Dabai, Chen Yi, Lü Bichou, and Chen Rong. Chairman was Tan Yankai. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) The Ministry of Interior proposed that according to a telegram from the Overseas Chinese United Association in Shanghai, a fire completely destroyed the Overseas Chinese residential area of ​​Pontianak, the capital of the western region of Dutch Borneo in the Nanyang region, on the 10th of this month, causing heavy casualties to the Overseas Chinese. It is extremely pitiful and should be allocated a large sum of money for relief. Is this appropriate? It was resolved that the government be requested to issue a clear order to the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to send consuls stationed there to investigate the disaster and comfort the victims. (2) The Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Health, and the Ministry of Transportation jointly submitted a report stating that they had been instructed to review the draft measures for inspecting mail and privately delivering narcotics presented by the Opium Prohibition Committee. Promulgation by the National Government - Regulations for Reorganizing the China Merchants Bureau

The National Government promulgated the provisional regulations for reorganizing the China Merchants Bureau on the 15th as follows: (Article 1) In order to reorganize the China Merchants Bureau to develop the national shipping industry, the National Government, in accordance with the resolution of the Second Plenary Session, has established a special committee to be solely responsible for supervision and guidance, and has established a general management office to appoint a commissioner to be responsible for the reorganization and management. (Article 2) The following matters shall be decided and implemented by the committee: (a) Determination of shipping policy (b) Abolition of affiliated institutions (c) Review and approval of the charter for appointment, removal, protection and service of staff (d) Increase of capital and settlement of equity (e) Review and approval of budgets and final accounts (f) Settlement of claims and debts (g) Distribution of profits (h) Conclusion and abolition of contracts (i) Custody and reorganization of property rights (j) Other important matters (Article 3) The committee shall consist of nine members selected and appointed by the National Government, and one person shall be appointed as chairman. (Article 4) The commissioner of the General Management Office shall be responsible for the overall management and reorganization of all affairs. (Article 5) The commissioner may attend committee meetings at any time to report on business conditions and present opinions. (Article 6) The committee shall establish a secretariat to handle committee affairs, a general audit office to be solely responsible for reviewing the receipts and expenditures of the general and branch offices and affiliated institutions, and compiling budgets and final accounts, and a design committee to be solely responsible for planning all reforms and financial reorganization methods of the bureau. The secretary-general, secretaries, directors of the audit office, members of the design committee, and all staff shall be appointed by the committee. (Article 7) The General Management Office shall establish a secretariat and various departments to handle bureau affairs. The secretary-general, secretaries, department heads, branch office directors, and directors of affiliated institutions shall be recommended by the commissioner and approved by the committee, and the remaining staff shall be appointed by the commissioner and reported to the committee for the record. (Article 8) The committee may appoint consultants to handle legal matters and provide consultation. (Article 9) The General Management Office may hire foreign experts for shipping, accounting, and other technical personnel. (Article 10) The committee shall submit a report to the National Government every six months on the business conditions, economic situation, and various business plans of the bureau, and the National Government may send personnel to inspect it when necessary. (Article 11) The organizational charter and rules of procedure of the committee, the organizational charter and rules of procedure of the general management office and branch offices, and the accounting and inspection rules shall be determined separately. (Article 12) If there are any matters not covered by these regulations, the committee may submit them to the National Government for amendment. (Article 13) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

The Communist Bandits' Second Attempt to Invade Changsha Fails

Changsha Correspondence: The communist bandits Zhu Mao, Peng Huang, etc., launched a full-scale invasion of Changsha on the evening of the 30th of last month, fighting fiercely for five days and nights until they were routed on the 4th of this month. Because the National Army held firm and waited for reinforcements, they did not pursue, so the bandit troops still occupied villages in the suburbs 30 to 40 li away. On the evening of the 10th of this month, Peng Huang, Zhu Mao, etc., again divided into four routes to invade Changsha, with Peng Dehuai's troops as the vanguard, launching a fierce attack on the positions of the National Army's right wing, including Ami Ridge, Yuhua Pavilion, Lannichong, Yangjiashan, Erlipai, Guitang, and Wujiaping. Peng Dehuai personally supervised the battle on the front line of Tiao Majian. The National Army defending the positions were the 16th Division of Peng Weiren and the New 5th Division of Gong Bingfan. The bandit army used fire oxen and big knife teams to advance in an attempt to destroy the power grid, followed by spear teams preparing for hand-to-hand combat, and then by rifle soldiers. Peng and Gong's divisions resisted with all their might, and for a time the sound of artillery was deafening and bullets rained down, with the fiercest fighting taking place around Yangjiashan and Ami Ridge. The communist bandits charged many times but were repelled. Because the power grid in front of the fortress had been increased to three layers, although the bandits charged fiercely and engaged in hand-to-hand combat, no one was able to break through the three layers. By 6:00 a.m. on the 11th, more than a thousand bandits had been killed and the bandit forces were unable to withstand the attack and retreated from the positions. The National Army still held its original positions and did not pursue. At dawn, it was seen that 600 to 700 people had been electrocuted and killed outside the power grid, and they were taken away by the Changsha County burial team for burial. At 8:00 a.m. on the 11th, He Jian personally went to Yangjiashan and Ami Ridge on horseback to inspect and comfort the officers and soldiers. As he was speaking to Peng's division, a crowd of bandits swarmed from the opposite mountain, Xiucai Slope, and attacked Yangjiashan. He Jian immediately personally supervised the battle and directed the artillery company to fire more than 20 shells. Airplanes also arrived in time and dropped more than 20 heavy bombs, killing hundreds of bandits. The bandits then retreated to the rear of the mountain. He Jian returned to the province on horseback at 1:00 p.m. Afterwards, the burial team found a paper order issued by Peng Dehuai on September 10 on the bodies of the dead bandits, stating that they would temporarily abandon the left wing and concentrate all their forces on the right wing to seize Changsha within three days from the evening of the 10th. Therefore, He Jian transferred Luo Lin's division, which was responsible for the left wing, to the right wing on the evening of the 11th to meet the enemy with strong forces, and waited in strict formation on the evenings of the 11th and 12th for the bandits to attack. However, the bandits did not attack for several days, presumably having fled far away. The victory reports of Peng and Gong's division commanders and Regiment Commander Liu are recorded below:

Report from Division Commander Peng Weiren: At about 9:00 p.m. on the 10th, more than 2,000 bandit troops advanced from the Dongshan area and attacked the positions of Regiment Commander Liu Jiren's 95th Regiment in the Ami Ridge area. When the bandits were 200 meters away from our positions, they used pine tree cannons to fire fiercely at Liu's troops. Regiment Commander Liu knew that they were earth cannons and remained hidden. It was not until the bandits were close that he realized that the bandits were attacking in four layers. The first layer was a big knife and axe team hoping to break through our power grid. The second layer was a spear team preparing to fight us hand-to-hand. The third layer was a machine gun and pistol team. The fourth layer was a rifle team. From 9:00 p.m. to dawn on the 11th, they charged our positions four or five times, advancing wave after wave with extreme intensity. Liu then used machine guns, bombs, and hand grenades to sweep the area, and the bandits were unable to withstand the attack and began to flee to the mountainous area in front of the Ami Ridge positions. Many bandits were killed in this battle, the number of which is countless, and several enemy flags were captured. One platoon leader and dozens of soldiers were also injured in our army. Report from Division Commander Gong Bingfan: (1) According to a report from Regiment Commander Yang Sizhong of the 20th Regiment, at 11:30 p.m. on the 10th, about 2,000 to 3,000 bandits used three machine guns to cover their advance to within dozens of meters of our positions in Wujiaping and attacked our Ami Ridge. After several hours of fierce fighting, more than 500 bandits were killed. The bandits were repelled at dawn on the 11th and Wujiaping was recovered. The bandits fled in a southeasterly direction. (2) According to a report from Regiment Commander Liu Zhenhan of the 17th Regiment, on the evening of the 10th, about 2,000 to 3,000 communist bandits attacked the Yangjiashan area. He led the 3rd Battalion to Yangjiashan to prepare for support. After careful investigation, our positions were heavily guarded and the bandits were unable to succeed. It was reported that the bandits moved to the Shiyanpu and Xujiaqiao areas.

Report from Regiment Commander Liu Jiren: At about 10:00 p.m. last night, the 10th, the communist bandits Zhu Mao and Peng Huang took advantage of the wind and rain to lead more than 10,000 of their main forces to attack our regiment's positions in Liujia Chong, Liangtui Chong, and Guitang. I immediately ordered the entire line to calmly meet the attack. Soon, the sound of the bandits' guns became louder and closer, and they attacked us fiercely. We also used machine guns to sweep the area. The bandits ignored everything and charged forward despite the bullets. At that time, the wind and rain were raging, not only could the sound of conversation not be heard, but one could not even distinguish one's fingers. Our officers and soldiers only used their hearing to measure the location of the bandits' gunshots and fired fiercely. Unexpectedly, the bandits were extremely cunning. All kinds of machine guns, submachine guns, and Mauser pistols were firing fiercely at us from about 100 meters in front of our positions. At the same time, a sabotage team armed with spears, sickles, and axes had crawled to our first iron fence, first throwing lime to try to obscure the vision of our soldiers. Then, the sound of knives, axes, and iron wire was heard. Our officers and soldiers immediately fired fiercely with machine guns, Mauser pistols, and submachine guns, and bombarded them with hand grenades. The bandits fled backwards, but returned again soon after, and were still repelled by us. They charged our iron fence more than ten times in this way, but never succeeded. Finally, Peng Huang and Zhu Mao personally led a pistol team and a machine gun company to attack our entire line fiercely. Bullets rained down and the firepower was extremely fierce. In a few minutes, several officers and more than a dozen soldiers in our regiment were injured. However, our morale was very high and we still fired calmly and fiercely at the bandits. Before long, the bandit troops charged forward towards us, and the sound of their shouts and the sound of gunfire were like a raging wind and angry tide. Our officers and soldiers used their superior fortifications to strike a heavy blow head-on, and their morale became stronger and stronger as they fought. The bandits finally collapsed and fled at dawn. In this battle, we killed more than 1,000 communist bandits, and the number of wounded was equal. In addition, about 300 people were drowned in the ponds of Liujia Chong and Liangtui Chong. Zhu Mao and Peng Huang suffered such a heavy loss that they were powerless to do anything. (September 13)

Gan Army Blocks Zhu Mao on the Hunan Border

Dai Yue's Brigade Defends on the Hunan-Jiangxi Border

Deng Ying's Division Destroys the Gujiang Bandit Nest

Nanchang Correspondence: Regarding the joint suppression of Zhu Mao and Peng Huang by the three provinces, the current focus is entirely on Hunan, with Jiangxi and Hubei playing an assisting role. Chief Commander Lu previously sent Jia Botao, the liaison officer of the 9th Route Army stationed in Jiangxi by the Wuhan Branch of the Executive Yuan, to Wuhan to consult with Director He on the specific plan for the joint suppression of the three provinces and report on everything. Jia has completed his mission and returned to Jiangxi to report to Lu. It is slightly heard that the joint suppression of the three provinces will still be carried out in accordance with the outline issued by Director He, and detailed methods will be drafted by each province and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and implementation. Chief Commander Lu is currently issuing orders to all counties in accordance with the outline for suppressing bandits in the three provinces, ordering them to establish defense groups, strictly implement rural cleansing, build blockhouses, and purchase guns for self-defense by the end of September, and to draft specific methods based on local conditions for approval and implementation.

Since the communist bandits of Zhu Mao and Peng Huang were repelled by the 4th Route Army and the Gonglu and other divisions in Changsha, the bandits have shown signs of fleeing from Liuyang and Liling towards the Jiangxi border. Border defense in Hunan and Jiangxi has become even more tense. Currently, Dai Yue's 52nd Brigade of the 18th Division is stationed in Wanzai to block and suppress the bandits from Liuyang. The 53rd and 54th Brigades have a part stationed in Shanggao and Pingxiang to intercept the bandits from Liling. The above units are setting up defenses step by step on the Hunan-Jiangxi border, waiting in strict formation. If the bandits attack, they will strike a heavy blow head-on. If necessary, they will advance from Pingxiang towards Liling and Zhuzhou to join the 4th Route Army. Liuyang has deep mountains and forests, and most of the people have been transformed into bandits, making it difficult to march. The Provincial Party Department previously sent a letter requesting Chief Commander Lu to suppress the bandits in Tonggu, Leping, and Yudu counties. Lu replied in a telegram: (The bandits are rampant, which is deeply regrettable. According to reports from various parties, I have ordered Ma's brigade to send troops to recover Yudu, and parts of the 18th Division and the 50th Division to suppress Leping, Jingzhen, and other places. Regarding the communist bandits in Tonggu, Brigade Commander Dai Yue has led a large army to station in Wanzai. Once the main force of Zhu Mao is annihilated, troops will be divided to suppress them severely.) and so on.

It can be seen that the province is currently concentrating its forces to deal with Zhu Mao.

Western Jiangxi has always been a den of communist bandits. While the main force is advancing to suppress Zhu Mao, the Red Army's pseudo-20th Army and pseudo-22nd Army have repeatedly laid siege to Ganzhou and Ji'an in an attempt to seize those two places and open up southern Jiangxi and western Jiangxi to respond to Zhu Mao. On the 4th of this month, the Red Army's independent regiment and the 123rd regiment joined forces with more than 10,000 peasant bandits from Anfu and Yongxin counties, armed with thousands of guns, and attacked the Zhenjun Mountain area near Jicheng with their main force. Division Commander Deng personally led his troops to fight. Regiment Commander Wang and Battalion Commander Hu also led their troops to charge bravely. In addition, the Luoshan police team launched a flank attack on the bandits' rear, and the bandits' line was thrown into chaos. Division Commander Deng took advantage of the victory to charge into the bandits' formation, killing 300 to 400 bandits. The bandits' regiment commander, Hu Xuejun, was also shot and killed. The remaining bandits scattered. Previously, the communist bandits launched a full-scale attack, and Division Commander Deng secretly ordered the security teams of Taihe, Xingguo, and Ji'an counties to attack the Gujiang bandit nest (located between Ji'an and Anfu, which has been occupied by the communist bandits since 1927). The bandits were caught off guard and were defeated by the security teams of various counties, suffering heavy casualties. The communist bandits' so-called wounded soldiers' government, Red Army school, and banks were all destroyed. The communist bandits are now in a dilemma. The communist bandits of the pseudo-22nd Army in southern Jiangxi have also been severely damaged by Ma's brigade and the security teams of various counties in Xinfeng and Yudu. Xinfeng has already been recovered, and Yudu will also fall soon. As for Fang Zhimin, the communist bandit who fled from eastern Jiangxi and disturbed Hukou and Duchang in northern Jiangxi, he has been defeated by the security regiment of Zhang Chao, the 1st and 2nd special task regiments of Wen Sen, and the 297th regiment of Yue Sen, and has retreated to the Duchang and Dexing areas. (September 13)

Hunan People Expand the Communist Eradication Movement

Changsha Correspondence: The communist bandits Zhu Mao and Peng Huang are currently retreating to the Jiumu, Daba Bridge, Jintuo, Luzhi Ridge, Tiao Majian, Tongjingpu, Datopu, Bantangchong, and Tianji Ridge areas 30 to 40 li away from Changsha, building fortifications and plotting a counterattack. Because the 4th Route Army and the Luo Lin and Gong Bingfan divisions must wait for the Gan army to concentrate on the Hunan border and the central government to send additional units to the Changsha-Yueyang area before launching another attack, they are currently holding the key fortresses in the suburbs of Changsha to consolidate the provincial defenses. In order to arouse the general public to work hard to eradicate the communists, the public groups of Hunan have organized the Hunan People's Communist Eradication Propaganda Committee, with Tang Yaozhang of the Provincial Party Department, Zhang Kailian of the Provincial Government, Du Yiwu of the Journalists' Association, Hu Yiru of the Provincial Education Association, Wang Jiansan of the Changsha County Party Department, Peng Zhuo of the Rural Cleansing Headquarters, Liao Zhengfan of the Garrison Headquarters, Liu Chaowu of the Changsha Municipal Public Security Bureau, Zhong Sun and Chen Guanghou of the industrial sector, Liu Houmin and Mao Bocun of the General Chamber of Commerce, and Feng Qingxun and Huang Zhaorong of the municipal regiment as committee members. It was officially established and the Hunan People's Expanded Communist Eradication Propaganda Week Conference was scheduled to be held at the Provincial Education Association on the 15th of this month. He Jian, Luo Lin, Gong Bingfan, etc. were appointed as the presidium of the conference and all institutions, groups, schools, and industries were notified to send at least 30 people each to attend the meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 15th. At the same time, each should organize at least one propaganda team of four people each, with one person as the team leader, to publicize the crimes of the communist bandits in the city and suburbs for one week from the 15th. Those who do not participate in the conference or organize propaganda teams will be deemed to be harboring the communists and will be severely punished.

In addition, the committee also stipulated five measures to expand the communist eradication propaganda, and sent them to all parties, with a unified deadline of completing them by the 14th. The measures are as follows: (A) Regarding all institutions and schools: the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" should be stamped on the envelopes and stationery. The style and location should be determined by each. (B) Regarding all stores: 1. The words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" must be stamped on invoices and wrapping paper. Invoices and wrapping paper that have already been printed must be stamped with a separate wooden stamp. 2. All possible methods must be used to engrave the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" on wooden packing boxes, cigarette tins, and metal boxes. 3. Nanhua stores should make "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" biscuits, following the method of "Never Forget National Humiliation" biscuits. The wrapping paper for mooncakes should also be stamped with the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists". 4. Ordinary envelopes and stationery sold by paper stores must be printed with the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists". 5. All kinds of books sold by bookstores must be stamped with the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" on the cover. 6. The measures used by grain stores must be stamped with the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron. 7. Money shops should stamp the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" with purple ink on common banknotes. (C) Regarding industry: 1. A square piece of galvanized iron should be nailed to the left handrail of rickshaws, painted with the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists". Each rickshaw puller should be issued a blue vest with white characters reading "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" to wear. The cost of clothing is borne by the rickshaw puller. 2. The carrying poles used by porters must be stamped with the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron. The words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" must be written around the baskets with ink. Each porter should be issued a blue vest with white characters reading "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" to wear. The cost of clothing is deducted from the rent of the baskets. 3. The tools used by mud and wood workers must be stamped with the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron on the wooden handles. 4. The capes used by barber shops must be stamped with the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" in purple. 5. All towel factories must weave the words "Eradicate the Communists" on the towels. 6. Tailors must stamp the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron on the back of their rulers. 7. Brush and ink stores must carve the words "Eradicate the Communists" on the brush handles and write the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" on the ink. 8. Boot and shoe businesses must stamp the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron on the shoe lasts. (D) Regarding the press: All newspapers should write the words "Work Hard to Eradicate the Communists" prominently before the editorials. (E) Regarding residents: Water buckets, rice steamers, baskets, carrying poles, carrying buckets, etc. must be stamped with the words "Eradicate the Communists" with a branding iron. The above five items must be completed before the 14th of this month, and the committee members will personally visit and inspect them at any time. Those who do not comply will be deemed to be harboring the communists and will be published in the newspapers and requested to be punished. (December 12)

Yan Xishan Goes to the Jinpu Railway to Comfort the Troops

His whereabouts are secretive and heavily guarded

Met an airplane on the way, but fortunately it did not drop bombs

Tianjin Correspondence: Since the outbreak of the military conflict, Yan Xishan has twice gone to the Jinpu Railway to command military affairs. The routes he took were different each time to avoid the central government's airplanes and bombs. On the afternoon of the 10th of this month, Yan Xishan prepared to go to the Jinpu Railway again. The Hebei area of ​​this city was placed under martial law early on the afternoon of that day at 6:00 p.m. At 4:00 p.m. that afternoon, Yan ordered the preparation of a special train. Xie Zongzhou, director of the Pinghan Railway Bureau, immediately prepared the train and parked it at the Dong Station in front of the gate. At 6:30 p.m., Yan ordered the train to return to Shijiazhuang, and Xie transferred the special train to the West Station. However, those with a little common sense of the current situation did not believe that he would return to Shijiazhuang. At 7:30 p.m., Kang Juyou, the battalion commander of the 1st Battalion of Yan's guard brigade, led the entire battalion of armed soldiers to board the train. It was originally intended to have a pilot train go ahead, but due to a lack of locomotives, it was merged with the special train, totaling 34 cars. At 8:00 p.m., soldiers, police, and military police arrived one after another and were heavily guarded, driving away idlers inside and outside the station. Even the duty officers and staff of the railway bureau had to wear uniforms, otherwise they were not allowed to wander on the platform. At 9:00 p.m., Yan went to Wang Jingwei's residence at No. 3 Hutong, Dongsi Pailou, to say goodbye. At 10:00 p.m., he returned to his residence to rest and drove his own red car No. 1 and No. 10 to the special train, with Chu Xichun, commander of the Beijing Garrison, and Wang Xifu, director of the Public Security Bureau, escorting him. At 11:00 p.m., Wang Jingwei, Tan Zhen, Xie Chi, Zhao Pilian, Zou Lu, and Ji Gongquan gathered again at No. 7 Hutong, Dongsi

Page 9

Summary of Important News

Pailou to see Yan off. Yan said that he was about to leave for the south to comfort the soldiers at the front, and asked Wang and Xie to be temporarily responsible for all party and government affairs. At 12:00 a.m., Wang and others left, and Yan prepared to depart. At this time, police were densely deployed on the roads from his private residence to Qianmen. Zhao Daiwen, Gu Renfa, Xie Zongzhou, and others boarded the train one after another. At 12:35 a.m., Yan arrived at the West Station, wearing a white summer cloth long shirt. A reporter asked Yan where he was going, and he replied that he could not say for sure. He was also asked whether Jia Jingde and Xue Dubi had reported to Beijing after contacting Zhang Xueliang in Shenyang, and he replied that no telegram had arrived in Beijing. He was asked when he would return to Beijing, and he replied that it would be in the near future. At 12:40 a.m., the special train departed. At 1:30 a.m., it arrived at Changxindian, and after the locomotive was watered, it turned into a branch road. At 6:00 a.m., it arrived in Tianjin. Yuan Qingzeng, commander of the Tianjin Garrison, and Zeng Yanyi, director of the Public Security Bureau, both came to the station to take care of the situation and temporarily mobilized security teams, pistol teams, broadsword teams, bicycle teams, and station military police to be on guard. The special train did not enter the station, and the locomotives were immediately changed. Liu Encheng, director of the Jinpu Railway Bureau, followed the train south. At 9:40 a.m., it arrived in Cangzhou, and the locomotive was watered. At 10:00 a.m., it drove south. At 1:20 p.m., it arrived in Dezhou. At 8:20 a.m. on the 10th, five red-tailed, white-winged airplanes were spotted circling over Yucheng for a week and dropped four bombs, all of which landed in open areas and caused no damage. The airplanes then returned south along the Jinpu Railway. At 10:40 a.m., another airplane was spotted over Cangzhou. The plane was very small and seemed to be a reconnaissance plane. At that time, Yan's special train was only 30 minutes away from Cangzhou and was spotted by the airplane. However, it was mistaken for a pilot train and continued to fly north for reconnaissance. When it reached Machang and did not see a train, it determined that Yan was on the first train and returned to Jinan to report, wanting to send bomber planes north again. Time was running out and Yan planned to get off the train in Pingyuan, but encountered the airplane on the way and got off the train in Dezhou instead, and his whereabouts are unknown. Zhang Yinwu heard in Yucheng that Yan had gotten off the train in Dezhou and took a special train to Dezhou to transfer to a car and chase after him. Based on this situation, it is speculated that Yan is in the vicinity of Dezhou. (September 12)

Duan Heng's Brigade Recovers Qiyang

Tang Shengming's Remnants Flee to Yongzhou

Changsha Correspondence: Tang Shengming, Li Zemin, Yan Renyi, Feng Tiangui, Wang Zuo, and other remnants of the Gui clique took advantage of the fact that the main force of the 4th Route Army was concentrated in Changsha to suppress the bandits and the south of Hunan was empty to successively seize Dong'an, Lingling, Qiyang, and other counties and invade Hengbao. He Jian ordered Duan Heng, the brigade commander of the 19th Division and commander of the Hunan Garrison, to lead his two regiments, Yu Gongqian and Chen Hanxiong, from Hengzhou along the Quanhu River to Qiyang to suppress the bandits, and ordered Luo Fanying, the division commander of the 16th Division (note that Luo has now been removed from his post and Peng Weiren has been promoted to division commander, but Luo has not yet handed over his duties and is still stationed in Baoqing), to sit in Baoqing, and to lead Luo's two regiments, Zhang Liangji and He Jingcheng, from Baoqing to Qiyang to attack. On the 7th, Duan's troops had reached Quanhu, and Luo's troops had reached Daying City, launching attacks simultaneously. After a day and night of fierce fighting, Battalion Commander Wang of Chen's regiment bravely charged into the positions of Tang Shengming's troops and killed the pseudo-brigade commander Chen Dunhe. The enemy's line wavered and retreated to Qiyang County. On the evening of the 8th, Chen's troops successively recovered Quanhu, Gaoling, and other places. At the same time, He Jingcheng's regiment also occupied Wenming City and Daying City on the 8th and killed an enemy regiment commander, Tang Shenghan. The enemy's entire line wavered and they abandoned Qiyang on the 9th and fled to Yongzhou and Dong'an. Chen Hanxiong's regiment of Duan Heng's troops then recovered Qiyang County on the 10th, and County Magistrate Tang Qiufan entered the city with the army on the same day to handle the aftermath. However, when the enemy troops withdrew from Qiyang, they looted the middle-class families, and none were spared. Brigade Commander Duan immediately entered Qiyang County on the 11th to plan the pursuit. Hengbao has turned from danger to safety. The people of Hengyang specially prepared wine, meat, incense, tobacco, and southern goods in the name of the Chamber of Commerce to send to the front line to comfort the officers and soldiers. After the recovery of Qiyang, it was heard that Brigade Commander Duan decided to divide into two routes to pursue: (1) Chen Hanxiong, Yu Gongqian, and other units will advance along the main road from Qiyang to Yongzhou. (2) Zhang Liangji, He Jingcheng, and other units will flank Yongzhou from Qiyang via Dong'an. Currently, each unit is advancing towards Yongzhou. (September 13)

Local Correspondence

Kunshan

Hunan Refugees Passing Through: Late one evening in front of Chaoyang Gate, more than three hundred male and female refugees from Hunan Province arrived. From among the refugees, Li and two others were chosen to request assistance from the county government. Upon learning of this, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched police to suppress them. That night, the refugees temporarily stayed in a temple. Yesterday morning, they were escorted out of the border by the police towards Taicang.

Rice Merchants Using Counterfeit Money: With the new grain harvest season approaching, rice merchants in this county, in order to compete for business, have made it a habit for years to send their staff with foreign currency to search for rice boats in the waterways at midnight. Around 3 a.m. yesterday morning, the Jixin Rice Shop outside Xiaoxi Gate sent its staff to Suzhou Tang to purchase a boatload of unpolished rice from Zhou Jingfu, a farmer from the countryside. At the time, they paid a deposit of ten yuan in Guangdong Bank exchange notes. They then instructed the farmer to send the rice to the shop, where it would be inspected before the final payment was made. Zhou took the deposit and sent the rice to the shop. By the time the rice was inspected, it was already dawn. Zhou, because the shop staff was too busy to settle the account, took the money to the market to buy goods. Someone noticed that the money was counterfeit and called the local police, who took Zhou to the public security police station. Zhou stated that the money came from the Jixin Rice Shop. The police went to the shop to investigate, which was confirmed. The shop owner, Zhu Pinxiang, was brought to the station, along with the farmer and the ten yuan in counterfeit money, and sent to the Ma Lu Public Security Bureau. The inspector, Su Xishan, interrogated them. Zhu Pinxiang stated that someone had come to the rice merchants' guild a few days ago offering to sell these banknotes for four yuan per hundred. He had purchased them to use for counting purposes and denied intending to use them as currency, adding that many merchants had bought them. Inspector Su, according to the statement, wondered what the rice merchants intended by buying such a large quantity of counterfeit money. He immediately sent a letter to the rice merchants' guild to inquire. The farmer was released as he was not involved. Zhu was temporarily released on bail by Xiang Daosheng, a staff member of the Zhangtai Rice Shop. Because the Rice Merchants' Guild has not yet provided a truthful response, the Ma Lu Public Security Sub-bureau submitted the case file to the main bureau on the 16th for a thorough investigation.

Qingpu

Clash Between Police and Shop Employee: On the 11th of this month, the Fourth Precinct Inspector Zhu Deshu of Chonggu Town received a report that there was gambling in Hefeng Lane. He immediately dispatched police to search everywhere but found no gambling or gambling equipment. After the police withdrew, they encountered Chen Fuquan, a debt collector from the Deyuan Rice Shop. Chen said that there had never been gambling in this area and there was no need to arrest gamblers. The tone was confrontational. The police officers beat him, causing injuries. Realizing they had caused trouble, they tore their own uniforms and falsely accused him of resisting arrest. They then arrested Chen Fuquan and took him to the bureau. The merchants of the town were greatly dissatisfied and convened a meeting of the chamber of commerce. They decided to publicly appoint representatives from various industries to petition the county government for a thorough investigation.

Suzhou

Appeal Hearing for Taikoo Stevedore Murder Case: Xiao Guirong, a stevedore at the Shanghai Taikoo Steamboat Wharf, picked a fight with his companion Su Guiting on April 30th of this year at 10:00 a.m., and beat Su Guiting, causing him to die from his injuries. Afterwards, Su's companion, Cai Arong, reported to the local security officer, Chen Liang, who requested the Shanghai Local Court to send personnel to conduct an autopsy and bring Xiao Guirong to court for investigation. At the conclusion of the trial, Xiao Guirong was sentenced to three years of imprisonment for the crime of intentional injury leading to death. Xiao, dissatisfied with the verdict, retained lawyer Pan Zhenya to appeal to the High Court. Yesterday (the 16th), Zheng Chi, the presiding judge of the Second Criminal Division of the High Court, conducted the hearing. The debate was concluded and a date was set for the verdict to be announced.

Chen Dezhou Falsely Accused of Being a Reactionary: Chen Dezhou, a native of Haimen, was carrying 1,835 yuan in banknotes last month, intending to go to Shanghai for business, when he was searched by the police chief of the Second Sub-bureau of the Haimen Public Security Bureau. 1,035 yuan in silver notes were confiscated. Another 800 yuan were hidden in the cart's box and were taken and escaped with by the cart pusher. Chen Dezhou was taken to the Second Sub-bureau. Later, someone suddenly accused Chen of being a reactionary and that the money he was carrying was intended to buy guns in Shanghai and return to his hometown to cause unrest. He was then transferred to the High Court here by the General Bureau. Yesterday (the 16th), the Second Criminal Division held a hearing. Lawyers Cai and Ni Pei appeared in court to defend Chen.

Commander Xiong Sets Deadline to Eradicate Lake Bandits: Xiong Shihui, the commander-in-chief for bandit suppression in the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, received a confidential report that the Pudong Lake Bandit gang, led by Taibao A Shu, had more than 500 bandits with 200 guns. They were currently roaming in the Dianshan Lake and Qianjiawei areas. He specially appointed Hu Zhengji as the temporary commander for bandit suppression in Qingjinping, commanding two infantry companies and one machine gun company from the 26th Regiment of the Fifth Division, and also commanding the First District of the Water Public Security and the First District of the Zhejiang Water Police to pursue and suppress the bandits relentlessly. If the lake bandits fled into the borders of Wujiang, Jinshan, Qingpu, Songjiang, Wuxian, Pinghu, Jiaxing, Jiashan, and other counties, the police teams from the Third District of the Water Public Security were to assist in the pursuit and suppression, with a deadline to eradicate them by the end of September.

Changshu

Execution of Notorious Bandit Liu Anbang: The case of the robbery and kidnapping of two men and women for ransom from the Gong Zifan family in Xizhou Market in this county last year resulted in the capture and execution by firing squad of a bandit named Liu Anquan. Later, another bandit named Liu Anbang was captured. After repeated court hearings, Liu admitted to robbing and kidnapping the Gong family. The county government telegraphed the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions on the Eastern date. The reply telegram stated that the bandit had confessed to robbery, kidnapping, and extortion, and should be executed. After receiving the telegram, the county executed the bandit by firing squad at the execution ground at 9:00 a.m. on the 15th after verifying his identity.

Wuxi

Victims of Economic Oppression: A certain Mrs. from a Yang Tiepi shop outside the West Gate of Xiyi, Cangbangli, recently became despondent due to the sluggish business in the shop and the increasing difficulty of making a living. Yesterday evening, she secretly went to the second vegetable market riverbank in that area and drowned herself. She died instantly, and her condition was very tragic. At the same time, a certain Jia from Jiangbei, who was in a grass shed near the Waidiaojiao Bridge, hanged himself in the shed because he could not make a living and was economically cut off. By the time his family discovered him, he had already passed away. It can be said to be tragic!

Robbery at Dasong Tomb: The Dasong Tomb near Zhangwang Temple outside the South Gate was originally a desolate place. Since the opening of the Yongtai and Yongchang silk factories, with workshops lining the area, it has become a lively market area. The night before last, Yan Ermei, a female worker from the Yongtai Silk Factory, was returning home from shopping at around 8:00 p.m. when she passed by the Dasong Tomb. Suddenly, two large men blocked her path, and another man held a pistol, threatening to shoot if she made a sound. They then robbed her of the gold bracelet on her wrist and the items she was carrying, totaling a loss of about eighty or ninety yuan. By the time the police were notified and began the pursuit, the thieves had vanished without a trace.

Pan Yichen Arrested for Being a Reactionary: The Capital Garrison Headquarters recently received a report that Pan Yichen, the current principal of Xin Du Bridge Elementary School, was engaged in reactionary activities. Yesterday, they sent detectives to Wuxi to directly contact the Wuxi Gendarmerie Regiment headquarters to jointly dispatch troops to the countryside and arrest Pan. He was taken to the city and briefly stayed at the Gendarmerie Regiment headquarters at the train station before being transported to Nanjing. Pan was formerly the principal of He La Kou Elementary School and was later hired as the director of the guidance department of Xiaozhuang Normal School Elementary School. This summer, Xiaozhuang was ordered to close, and Pan also returned to Wuxi. This time, he was falsely accused. The educational community is now trying to find ways to rescue him.

Sun Junxiu Regains Freedom: Sun Junxiu, the former propaganda minister of the County Party Headquarters, was detained by the High Court on suspicion of counter-revolutionary activities. Later, due to the Tan Qixuan massacre case, Tan's family accused Sun of instigating the crime. He was transferred back from Suzhou for trial. After repeated interrogations and prolonged delays, Sun's sentence for the counter-revolutionary part had already been served. There was also no concrete evidence in the Tan case. Recently, Lu Aijie, a member of the Case Clearance Committee, opened a trial and determined that Sun Junxiu was definitely not involved in the Tan case and ordered him to be released on bail.

Strict Investigation of Large Quantities of Shaanxi Opium: The Wuxi Station Police Subdivision received a telegram yesterday from the Police Department of the Jinghu Railway Bureau, stating that they had discovered that the enemy was secretly transporting 1,500 large packages of Shaanxi opium, worth over 300,000 yuan, to Shanghai for transshipment to the interior, including Suzhou and Wuxi. They were ordered to pay attention to the investigation. The police subdivision chief has ordered the police to strictly investigate.

Changzhou

Robbery and Fatal Injury of Victim in the Ninth District: Zhuang Yanming's family, the head of Wushang Township, Dajiang Village, near Dong'an Town in the Ninth District of Wuyi, was suddenly attacked by more than ten armed bandits at around 9:00 p.m. on the 14th. All family members were tied up, and Xiang Da, Yanming's father, was forced to reveal the location of hidden money. Xiang Da could not comply, and the bandits stabbed him three times in the body with a knife. At the same time, they fired a handgun at him, hitting his head three times, killing him instantly. The bandits searched wantonly and then fled towards Butou Town.

Key Criminals in Kidnapping Case Cracked at West Gate: Chen Dianming, a boatman at the West Gate of Wuyi, was suddenly approached by Zhang Jinbiao and others the other day, who forcibly demanded a loan of silver. When their demands were not met, they kidnapped Chen's young son, Chen Xiaor. Chen's son managed to escape during an opportunity. Chen Dianming seized Zhang Jinbiao and reported the case to the responsible Public Security Precinct, requesting an investigation. Inspector Xu, considering the case to be a kidnapping, immediately led a team to investigate in different directions. They successively captured accomplices Dang Kaqin, Bian Jigen, and Jin Xiaozhuzi. Bian Jigen was a repeat offender in robbery cases and was also a key criminal in the Town robbery case. When he was arrested, a bomb and several other items were found in his home. After interrogation, he confessed to the robberies. Inspector Xu obtained the confession and, along with the witnesses, sent the individuals to the County Law Office on the afternoon of the 15th for handling.

Jiangyin

Li Hongze and Others Escorted to Province for Interrogation: Li Hongze, the dismissed inspector of the Public Security Bureau, was involved in the case of falsely issuing a pistol with the Yin character. He, along with Xu Yongliang, Xu Yun, and Li Rongbao, plotted to kidnap the son of Tan Nanshan of Changshou. The case was reported by the County Party Headquarters. Li, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, telegraphed the Wuxi Public Security Bureau to detain Li Hongze and summon Xu Yun and the other three as witnesses. Xuan Jibao and patrol officers Chen Peiyang and Cao Shichu were brought to the case. Yang, the presiding investigator, interrogated them four times. Subsequently, So-and-so and others accused Xu Yongliang and others to the provincial government of privately possessing firearms and requested strict punishment. Based on the situation, the provincial government believed that the truth of the matter should be thoroughly investigated. It specifically instructed County Magistrate Li of Jiangyin to collect all case files and escort Xu Yongliang and the other four to the province for interrogation. After receiving the order on the morning of the 15th, County Magistrate Li instructed bailiff Wu Bowen and bailiff Liu Xiangting to escort them to the province. The Provincial Government Guard took them to the press room to be guarded overnight. Yesterday morning (the 16th), they were transferred to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for processing.

Zhenjiang

Wounded Soldiers Management Committee Arrives in Zhenjiang for Inspection: Shao Weihan, the commander of the Second Group of the Capital Wounded Soldiers Welfare Committee and Jinghu Road, arrived in Zhenjiang the night before last to inspect the wounded soldiers. Yesterday morning at 4:00 a.m., he specially led a platoon of military police from the Guard Brigade and a platoon from the First, Second, and Third Groups of the Inspection Division and the Public Security Team to the Eighteenth Rear Hospital outside the South Gate to inspect the hospitalized wounded and sick soldiers. A total of 184 wounded soldiers who had recovered were inspected. Dai, the head of the Fourth Group of the Inspection Division, led a platoon to escort them to the capital. Commander Shao then took a boat to Yangzhou on the same day to inspect the 800 recovered wounded soldiers in Yangzhou, who were also transported to Zhenjiang today for transshipment to the capital to work at the front. It is heard that Shao also plans to travel from Yangzhou to Nantong.

Various Circles Discuss Fushou Nunnery Case: Monk Hongkai, the former abbot of Fushou Nunnery, did not abide by the monastic rules. After discussions by various local organizations, it was decided to expel him from the country and confiscate the temple property to subsidize local autonomy projects. Recently, the monk suddenly returned to Zhenjiang and filed a lawsuit in the local court to restore the temple property. Yesterday, representatives from various circles held a second joint meeting and decided to send a letter to the county government to expel him again, with the temple property to be permanently transferred to the local government for public undertakings.

Court Issues Arrest Warrants for Two Fugitives: Hui Wu, the leader of a gang of kidnappers detained in the detention center of the local court, and Wang Lianfu, a repeat offender of opium trafficking who had been convicted, escaped through a window at 4:00 a.m. the day before yesterday. The court issued a reward notice yesterday for their arrest.

Self-Defense Corps Disperses Bandits: At about 9:00 p.m. on the afternoon of the 14th, more than thirty bandits suddenly came to Huocun in the southern countryside of the county, surrounded the village, and searched house by house. Neighboring villages heard the alarm and gathered the Self-Defense Corps to drive away the bandits. After the incident, it was investigated that the Yuan and Zhao families had been looted, suffering considerable losses.

Nantong

Nantong and Four Other Counties to Implement Rural Clearance: Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Taixing, and Jingjiang counties have received a provincial order to implement rural clearance according to the Taihu Lake area model. The five counties fear that businesses will decide to proceed simultaneously and complete the project within three months.

Implementation of Combination in Reclamation Areas: The Yannan, Yancheng, and Nantong prefectures of Huainan feel various difficulties recently and are negotiating to combine into a unified organization to actively defend themselves and seek the progress of the reclamation business. The plan has been drawn up in recent days and will soon be decided jointly by representatives from each district.

Gaoyou

Suspicious Military Officer Escorted to Province for Disposition: The Seventh Company of the Postal Security Team stationed in Youjia arrested two men at the Zhonghua Building the night before last, Zhang Zhengkun, who claimed to be the commander of the Xuzhou-Huaihai Guerrilla Supplement Regiment, and Dai Wenbiao, a special agent. They were then sent to the county government. After Secretary Qiang briefly questioned them in court, they were handed over to the Public Security Bureau for custody because they did not have a formal official document ordering them to recruit soldiers in Youjia. It is now heard that County Magistrate Wang ordered the First Squadron of the Police Bureau last night to escort Zhang and Dai to the Zhenjiang Security Department for disposition.

Public Security Branch Chief Accused of Thorough Investigation: Liu Hongtao, the chief of the First Public Security Branch in the county-affiliated Sanduo Town, is now being sued by the town's citizens, Jin Zifan and others, in the county government, accusing him of harboring opium and extorting money from the people. County Magistrate Wang ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate and reply. It is now heard that Director Zhang has commissioned Section Chief Wei Guo Baoheng of the Second Section to conduct a thorough investigation.

Kidnapping Case at Xiaotang River: At about 9:00 p.m. the night before last, six or seven bandits suddenly came to the home of Wu Jichang, a farmer in Xiaotang River of the county, broke in through the door with guns, and kidnapped his son, daughter-in-law, and granddaughter. They demanded a ransom of 1,000 yuan, otherwise they would not only execute the hostages but also set fire to the house. It is now heard that Wu has reported the case to the county government, requesting strict investigation.

Jiashan

Robbery Leads to Three Deaths: The home of Wang Hesheng, a farmer in Chendoubang, Dingzha District of the county, earned just enough to make ends meet. Late last night, more than ten bandit boats suddenly arrived with more than twenty bandits armed with electric torches and cannons. They rushed into Wang's house, kidnapped a seven-year-old girl, and wounded Wang Yousheng with a knife. They shot and killed a worker named Amu. This morning, the girl's body was found in the Tan Beach. The family went to retrieve it and bury it.

Xiaoshan

The Repercussions of a False Accusation of Adulterated Rice: Yao Fumao's rice shop outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan was accused by Wang Weishan, an unemployed grocery store employee, of adulterating new rice. He extracted a sample of rice and reported it to the Party Headquarters, which forwarded a letter to the county government for investigation. The shop owner of Yao Fumao was summoned to court for interrogation and judgment on the 12th. It is now learned that the rice industry colleagues are greatly dissatisfied with Wang Weishan's unfounded accusations that damage the reputation of the industry. More than twenty rice shops have jointly submitted a petition to the county government requesting a thorough investigation of the false accuser to serve as a warning against troublemakers.

Provincial Order for Early Rice Rent Payment Measures: The Xiaoshan County Government believes that many new lease agreements in the county's tenancy industry have not been established. The method of on-site supervision of rent collection has not been carried out in accordance with legal procedures, as evidenced by past facts last year. Now that the early rice harvest season has arrived, remedial measures should be stipulated. It is now learned that County Magistrate Du received instructions from Min Ying yesterday, allowing the use of estimation methods. The villages and neighborhoods should reliably estimate the standards and report them to the county for approval and forwarding for filing. It has now been forwarded to the District Offices and Township Preparatory Offices for compliance and public notice.
