Ministry of Education Investigates Overseas Chinese Schools

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed all overseas consulates to report the overseas Chinese school investigation forms within a deadline of one and a half months. The original order stated: "It has been found that the overseas Chinese school investigation forms have been distributed by this ministry, requiring the completion of the investigation within the shortest possible time and ordering prompt filling and reporting. It has been found that this time the forms have either not been investigated and reported to this ministry or, although they have been reported, they are not complete. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby ordered that the consulates submit the said forms to this ministry within one and a half months of the date of this document, so that statistics can be compiled."

Yunnan Donglu University to be Changed to Provincial Status

Yunnan Private Donglu University was founded by Tang Jiyao. The name Donglu was based on the alias that Tang held which meant "East Mainland master", and so he honored himself. The school was established in the 12th year of the Republic of China. The school site was rebuilt and merged with the provincial Jia Grade Industrial School. Departments such as literature, civil engineering, mining, and metallurgy were established. The curriculum was based on the availability of teachers, so many courses were incomplete and rudimentary. Tang Jiyao was responsible for raising funds, and there was no dedicated fund. In the early days of its establishment, the funds were still sufficient, but after Tang's death, fundraising became extremely difficult. The person in charge, a Dong who was Tang's brother-in-law, had no ability to raise funds and was also inconvenient to request to be changed to provincial status, so it was almost impossible to maintain. It was found that the school had not applied for registration and had not complied with the Ministry regulations. Now the Ministry of Education is actively cracking down on private universities and reorganizing provincial universities. It has telegraphed the Yunnan Education Department to present and verify the nature of Donglu University. According to the Yunnan Education Department's telegram yesterday, "Having received the order, we immediately submitted it to the provincial government for discussion and decided to reorganize the private Donglu University into Yunnan Provincial University, which will be implemented in the next semester." This means that the school has been decided by the provincial government to be changed to a provincial university.

Ministry of Education Urges Dispatch of Funds for Beiyang Institute of Technology

Cai Yuanze, the president of Beiyang Institute of Technology, previously telegraphed the Ministry of Education to resign due to the shortage of funds at the institute, which made it difficult to maintain operations. The Ministry of Education telegraphed to comfort him. According to a telegram from the president in Tianjin, "Minister Jiang, I respectfully acknowledge receipt of the telegram. I am greatly relieved to hear that the meeting on the 9th approved 20,000 yuan. Although the lights and water have been cut off, I will still comply with the order to maintain operations. Please telegraph the funds as soon as possible to alleviate the urgent need." It is heard that the Ministry of Education has urged the Ministry of Finance to dispatch the funds to provide relief.

Recent News from Jiangsu Teacher Training Correspondence Department

Graduates have service opportunities

Non-graduates have new remedial measures

Second session of students scheduled to start classes

The Teacher Training Correspondence Department attached to the Jiangsu Provincial Preparatory Office for Joint Compulsory Education has held graduation ceremonies for the first session of students, issued certificates, and sent a list of names to the education bureaus of various counties for priority employment. It is reported that all have considerable service opportunities. It is also learned that the graduates of the department have the qualifications to serve as substitute elementary school teachers in accordance with the instructions of the Provincial Department of Education. Eighty to ninety percent of the students who participated in the teacher certification examination in the last session have been admitted as full-time teachers and are ranked among the top. This is because the test subjects are completely related to the department's usual study subjects. Having been prepared, the admission is guaranteed. The department's examination results are always strict. In order to take care of the first session of non-graduating students, new training methods have been formulated. Homework guidance and research questions will still be issued in installments to urge students to answer in detail and record them in notebooks for the department to review. At the same time, itinerant instructors will be hired to guide them in various counties. Those who pass the make-up examination in the future will be allowed to reissue graduation certificates. Now, in response to the needs of various counties, the second training session has been continued. The education bureaus of various counties have recommended students from as many as thirty-eight counties, with more than six hundred students. Classes are scheduled to begin on September 25th. The lectures in this session will adopt progressive methods, with schools as the unit, progressing gradually and detailing research methods on a regular basis, combining the three aspects of doing, learning, and teaching. The content of the lectures is particularly precise and essential.

Nine Articles of Jiangsu Teacher Training Correspondence Continued Training Measures (1) First session non-graduating students will be allowed to participate in the second session of teacher training correspondence department continued training in accordance with these measures (2) Except for those not changed, the other lectures on revised and newly added various subjects will be reissued (3) In order to increase learning efficiency, the progressive method will be adopted according to the subject, and homework guidance instructions and research methods for each subject will be issued along with the second training department (4) Newly compiled research questions will be issued separately for each subject, and students should record detailed answers to the questions in notebooks and submit them to this department for review (5) In addition to being guided by itinerant instructors at any time, students who encounter difficult problems in their studies may also fill in problem papers (which will be sent by the correspondence department) to request answers from this department (6) Regular tests and graduation exams must be attended this time and must not be neglected (7) Other guidance matters are generally the same as those of the second session students (8) Those who pass the examination will be allowed to reissue graduation certificates (9) Students who volunteer to participate in the continued training should fill in and send a volunteer form and resume form, along with a tuition fee of four yuan, to the local education bureau for collection and submission to this department before September 20th before they can be admitted

Local News

Ministry of Education Recognizes Fudan Student Qualifications

The Ministry of Education approved the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's consultation regarding Fudan University graduates applying for certified public accountant certificates and requesting proof of their qualifications. The Ministry of Education stated that the school had been registered by the former Beijing Ministry of Education and the University Council and was in compliance with the Ministry's No. 8 Announcement on the recognition of measures and should be recognized. The Ministry of Education specifically replied to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating that it approved your ministry's consultation regarding Gong Fangzhong, Xu Wu, and Lu Zuoyun applying for the issuance of certified public accountant certificates and requesting proof of their Fudan University graduation qualifications. Fudan University was approved for registration by the former Beijing Ministry of Education in August of the 14th year and was approved for registration by the former University Council in October of the 17th year. According to the Ministry's No. 9 Announcement of this year, the recognition of the qualifications of graduates of private secondary schools and above that have been approved for registration by the former Beijing Ministry of Education is limited to those who graduated before July 23rd of the 17th year for specialized schools and above. The school was invalid only during August and September of the 17th year. No graduation should have been held during this period. All graduates of the school, except those who graduated from schools approved for recognition by the former Beijing Ministry of Education, should be handled in accordance with the recognition measures stipulated in the Ministry's No. 8 Announcement of this year if the school level at the time of graduation is equal to the school level at the time of recognition. All others do not need to go through recognition procedures. This is the corresponding reply.

6:30 AM

Chinese Expedition Football Team Returns to Singapore from Medan

Sixteen players currently in the team || Awaiting telegrams from the West before setting sail

Four wins out of four in Medan || Li Huitang scores eleven goals alone

(Singapore Dispatch, September 6) The main purpose of the Chinese expedition football team's trip to Southeast Asia is to organize a Chinese football expedition team to tour Europe. This has been reported in the newspapers, and readers should already be aware. On August 20, when the team returned to Singapore from Java, the reporter reported the news obtained, saying: "(...) The team's trip to Europe was originally scheduled for August 22 by British mail, but yesterday a telegram came from London instructing them to postpone the departure by fourteen days, because the ship of the next group is scheduled to leave Singapore on September 6." Today, September 6, has arrived. If it can be done, they will overcome all obstacles and ride the long winds and break the waves of thousands of miles! However, on August 25, the team also accepted the invitation of people from Medan in the Dutch East Indies to play four matches in Medan, and they could only finish the competition and return to Singapore on the second of the month. The time difference from the original scheduled departure date for Europe is not much. According to speculation, the team will definitely arrive in Singapore and then depart. Yesterday (5th), although the team had already returned to Singapore, there was still no intention of leaving. The reporter made a special visit to inquire about the news of the European trip. It was found that the team of fifteen people were all staying on the third floor of the South Heaven Hotel, in a total of four rooms. The reporter arrived and went to Room 33 on the third floor to meet Mr. Ma Yuheng, the team leader, and learned that their trip to Europe still had to wait for a telegram from London, so the original plan to depart on a British ship in the next few days could not be fulfilled. They are currently staying at the South Heaven Hotel temporarily. After the Chinese team leaves Singapore to return to Hong Kong this afternoon (6th), they will move to Mr. Hu Wenhu's villa in Pasir Panjang to live. The area there is extremely quiet, which is most suitable, and cannot be compared with the noisy South Heaven. As for the future trip to Europe, Mr. Chen Mei'an from Ipoh and Mr. Ya Jiu, Ya Hui, and Wen Li from Singapore will all accompany them. Mr. Chunlin has not yet been decided. The team currently has a total of thirteen warriors in Singapore, plus Chen Meian, Ya Jiu, Ya Hui, and Wen Li, totaling sixteen people. They still need to find two or three more people to join them to strengthen their strength. As for the results of this trip to Medan in the Dutch East Indies, they were excellent. They played four matches and did not draw or lose any of them.

According to Mr. Yu, in the first match in Medan, the result of the match against the Chinese team was three to two. The Dutch people there made a great criticism, thinking that Lehua was only famous in name. The Chinese newspapers said that the visiting team gave way a bit at first, which was the most polite thing to do. By the second time, they fought fiercely with the Sudong team, which was recognized by the local people as the strongest team and had drawn with the Singapore Army team, and they defeated them with eight to one. As a result, the Dutch newspapers reported it widely, saying that the team was completely different from before, and the third and fourth matches were like entering an uninhabited area, and the opponents all fled without gaining anything. In the four matches, they scored a total of sixteen points, and the "ball monster" Mr. Li Huitang alone scored twelve points. His power shook Sudong Island, which can be imagined! Mr. Li Huitang's old illnesses from Shanghai to Singapore to Java had not yet healed, so his performance was mediocre. Not only did it disappoint the audience, but he himself also regretted it. Calling him a "ball monster" is very appropriate. After arriving on Sudong Island, his strange power recovered, so he had this achievement. The team is currently waiting for a telegram from London in Singapore, as mentioned above. Mr. Yu said that if there is an opportunity, they will meet with the Singapore United team again and play a strong match. If there is a longer time (about ten days), they plan to travel to places such as Malacca and Ipoh, because the team stayed in Singapore the longest after arriving in Malaya, and only went to Kuala Lumpur for a few days. After the reporter finished talking with Mr. Yu, he said goodbye and left.

Four Wins Out of Four in Medan

The Chinese Expedition Football Team's four wins out of four in Medan are listed on the left:

Date Opponent Score Goals Scored by Li Huitang

August 27 Wins Chinese 3 to 2 2

August 29 Wins Sudong 8 to 1 6

September 1 Wins Dutch League 3 to 0 1

September 2 Wins Wu League 2 to 0 2

Detailed Account of the 2-0 Victory over Wu League

(Medan Dispatch, September 2) After the Chinese Expedition Football Team arrived in Medan, they won four consecutive victories. After defeating the Dutch League 3-0 on the 1st of this month, they defeated the Wu League 2-0 on the 2nd. The details are as follows: The audience in the stadium on the day of the match was no less than before, especially Malays, accounting for more than half. There were also many Chinese, followed by Europeans and Westerners. It was an unprecedentedly lively scene. At the sound of the bell at five o'clock, the notary blew the whistle to gather the five teams. After the site was selected, a silver whistle was heard, and the two sides began to fight. First, the Chinese team kicked off, but the Wu League's forwards were blocked by the Wu League's center forward, who dribbled the ball up. At the same time, the left and right wings provided remote cover, and the midfielders also rushed to meet the Chinese team's center forwards and midfielders. The left and right guards rushed to grab and seize the ball. The momentum was very fierce. In addition, most of the Wu League's warriors were elite and were also new forces, so at this time, although the Chinese team had the nimble pioneer Dai and the brave General Cao, it was difficult to win for a while.

(I) Li Huitang's Futile Efforts

At 5:10, Li Huitang rode alone, seized a ball, and dribbled it up. Unfortunately, he was besieged by the Wu League's forwards and defenders, and the Chinese team's forwards could not rush to him in time, so he was isolated and helpless. He was eventually counterattacked by the League's center forward. The ball fell to the Chinese team. Sun Sijing passed it to the left wing, and Chen Guangyao shot it with one foot, but it passed diagonally over the Wu League's goal, so he missed a good opportunity.

After the Wu League's goal kick, the Wu League's warriors, seeing the Chinese team's fierce grabbing and shooting methods, had no choice but to adopt guerrilla tactics to try to win. Therefore, whenever the ball fell to the Chinese team, they would rush out from all directions and use two-way attacks to attack one of the Chinese team's generals. Although they could not penetrate the Chinese team's goal, the Chinese team's line often shook because of this. When the battle reached 5:15, the Wu League fiercely shot another ball, which fell to the Chinese team's second line of defense. At this time, the Chinese team's midfielders were empty, and several Wu League warriors had already rushed to the ball, which fell to the Wu League's record line. The Chinese League was able to turn danger into safety.

(II) Zhou Xianyan Forcefully Repels the Mighty Army

When Li Ning cleared the ball, the ball fell into the Wu League's camp and was shot from the side by the Chinese team's forward Dai Linjing and dribbled by the right wing Cao Guicheng to the Wu League's border area, right in the middle of the Wu League's goal. Unfortunately, it was blocked by the Wu League's goalkeeper. Then, there was another melee. The two sides charged several times. The Wu League was not afraid of guns, charging straight and ramming into the Chinese team. In order to preserve its strength, the Chinese team did not want to make unnecessary sacrifices. At 5:25, who knew that the ball was shot by the Wu League's center forward and rebounded. Fortunately, it was kicked away by Zhang Shilong with one foot, but the Wu League regrouped and came back again. Even the Chinese team was surrounded, and the goal was in danger. At 5:27, the Wu team actually got a ball and rushed to the goal. Fortunately, the Zhou Iron Gate was quick-witted and grabbed it and counterattacked it in the Wu League's defense line. Before long, the notary blew the whistle to rest, and the first half ended in a draw.

(III) Three Attacks Fail to Achieve Success

After the five-minute break, the victory or defeat of the two armies was entirely dependent on the thirty minutes of the second half. Initially, the Wu team's center forward kicked off and passed it to the front left forward, who slanted and dribbled it with the right wing guard. He was met head-on by the Chinese team's left wing Chen Guangyao. Then, Chen Guangyao shot and sent it to the center forward. Dai Linjing obtained it and passed it to Chen Tian, but in the end, the Wu League's warriors from all directions arrived and the ball was scattered. At 5:41, the ball monster Li Huitang stepped out from the crowd, received a ball, and shot it at the Wu League's goal, but unfortunately, it was received by its goalkeeper, who seemed to be in pain, and reluctantly kicked the ball away. At 5:45, Li Huitang dribbled another ball, and just as he was about to shoot, he was scattered by the Wu League's forwards. Finally, at 5:46, Cao Guicheng passed a ball, and Li Huitang dribbled it up, slaying generals and entering, breaking through two passes in a row. When he reached the Wu League's second line of defense, he lifted his foot and the ball flew from the side of the Wu League's goal, but to no avail. The audience shook their heads and sighed.

(IV) The Onlookers Sigh Secretly

After the ball monster Li Huitang fiercely shot at the Wu League's goal three times without success, the Chinese audience in the whole stadium, seeing that the Wu League was brave but lacked strategy, but its strength could not be underestimated, and seeing that the time for the truce was approaching and the victory or defeat was still undecided, for the sake of the face of the compatriots, the honor of China, and the glory of the country, they were all worried and sighed secretly. The sincerity of the compatriots in protecting China can be seen here.

However, the Wu League also saw that the Chinese team had not been able to win in these five minutes, and thought of launching a major counterattack to seek the final victory. At the same time, the goalkeeper firmly defended the base camp, the defenders also attacked, and the forwards were all dispatched to the Chinese team's position. At this time, the Chinese team used a method of continuous flaws in attack and defense to break the League's formation, attacking and seizing each other. The Chinese team was besieged twice, like a stream of water that could not be discharged. The left side was blocked, and the right side came again. Many of them were knocked back by Li Ning's head. At this time, although the Wu League used brute force, it was not as rude and irritable as the Dutch League team the day before, secretly releasing cold arrows. In this respect, the Wu League was better than the Dutch League after all.

(V) Good Luck Brings Continued Victory

The two sides fought each other until 6:05, when with a thunderous sound, General Li, who was accurate in every shot, suddenly burst out with energy, rushed forward bravely, and used his magical art of passing through several enemies with one body. The Wu League's forwards were exhausted to cope. Before long, Liang Rongde passed in a ball, and Li Huitang immediately took the opportunity to use a half-lying shooting method, and with a swish, the ball flew into the Wu League's goal from behind. At the same time, the applause and the sound of firecrackers celebrating the victory were like mountains collapsing and the earth cracking. The compatriots had turned their worries into joy. When the battle resumed, the morale of the League and Wu teams was shaken by this defeat, and the courage to counterattack also plummeted. Therefore, the ball was often in the Wu League's second line of defense at this time. Although it was kicked back by the defenders several times, the forwards did not respond. At 6:08 (only two minutes away from the truce), the Chinese team's Chen Tian dribbled a ball and passed it to the center forward line for Li Huitang to dribble towards the Wu League, breaking through the second line of defense. When he lifted his foot, the ball flew and went into the net again. The applause thundered again. After rearranging the formation and fighting again, the two sides fought in a melee for two minutes, but there was no progress. Then, the notary blew the whistle to end the game. As a result, the score was two to zero, and China won again.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

A: There's a powder magazine here; you can't smoke. Didn't you hear about the tragedy last month when someone smoking a cigarette here caused an explosion that killed twelve people?

B: But that won't happen today.

A: Why?

B: Because there are only you and me here.

A: Woman, what are you doing here?

B: Searching for my husband.

A: Don't you already have a husband?

B: That's why I have to go out and look for him so often.

Doctor: What's wrong? Are you suffering from insomnia again? You should eat something every night before you go to sleep.

Patient: But the last time I came to see you, you told me not to eat anything.

Doctor: That was three months ago. Don't you know that medicine is constantly progressing? So, before, you didn't have to eat anything before going to bed, but now you must eat.

Teacher (reproaching an unpromising student): Child, why are your grades always lagging behind?

Student: Only when you lag behind can you catch up and make progress. So, I always let people make the first move.

Anecdotes about Mr. Yuan Guanlan

— Zhang Limin

The senior educator, Mr. Yuan Guanlan of Baoshan, unfortunately passed away from illness last month. From then on, another educator in Jiangsu has weakened. It is truly regrettable. Recently, someone from Baoyi came and said that Mr. Yuan was outstanding in writing, excelling in both traditional and modern styles. His writings were all pertinent and were admired by us younger students. He was also skilled in speech. Whenever he participated in group organizations, agencies, and conferences, the audience was always fascinated by his speeches when he took the stage. I remember in the spring of the 18th year of the Republic, when the Jiangsu Tongzhi Compilation Committee convened a conference to discuss the gazetteer's outline, Mr. Yuan, as an advisor to the committee, was also present. I am recording his speech regarding the editing of the astronomy section: "According to the relationship between the local area and the stars, there was the so-called 'field division' in the past, which assigned the twelve states in the country to the constellations in the Zhou Tian two times. Before the Han Dynasty, many scholars had disputes about the distribution and the beginning and end of the degrees. After examining the modern scientific method of actual measurement, there is nothing that can be connected. However, in the past few decades, the gazetteers of the provinces and counties have mostly followed this and have not changed it. It is truly like still wearing a fox fur in the hot summer. It is extremely out of touch with the times. I urge you to remove this ancient saying of field division and not include it. Please do not be like wearing fur clothes in the hot summer and not taking them off, causing criticism for sweating but not exerting effort."

Mr. Yuan had a tall and extraordinary appearance, and his throat sound was like that of a woman returning home, which was also very rare.

A Record of Intelligent and Courageous Sisters

— Huang Yingdai

There is a family with the surname of Mou in Zhangzhishan Town, Nanxiang, Nantong. The family is well-off and only has a father and two daughters. The elder sister is slightly older and is betrothed to a son of the Mou family in the same village as his wife. The wedding is scheduled for this winter, and the dowry and other items are being prepared. Many of the clothes and other items have also been made. Since the father has no sons, he will naturally give a particularly generous dowry when he marries off his eldest daughter. Unexpectedly, the hired seamstress saw so many silk clothes and harbored greedy intentions. One night, the father happened to be out on business and stayed overnight at a relative's house. The seamstress knew that the younger sisters were at home and were not to be feared, so she invited three or four people to go to their house late at night, hoping to steal all the wedding clothes. After arriving at their house, they broke in. The sisters heard the noise and knew that there were bandits. They were not too flustered. The elder sister stood at the door and saw a thief entering the room. She immediately grabbed him with her hands and resisted him. Her younger sister saw this and thought of helping her sister. Suddenly, she saw a large iron scale next to the door of the room. In a moment of desperation, she grabbed the scale bar and pretended to fire a gun at the thief, and twisted the iron button and iron hook at the end of the scale to make it sound like the mechanism on a gun. The thief could not tell the difference in the dark. Seeing the scale bar aimed at his face, he thought it was a real gun. He quickly turned his head and ran out desperately. The three accomplices were terrified and began to question the seamstress, who had instigated them. She had said that there were no guns in the Mou family's house. Under the cross-examination, the seamstress could not defend herself for a while, but she still could not fully believe it. The next morning, she went to the Mou family's house to work and learned the whole story of how the sisters had used the scale bar to repel the thieves the night before. She told her accomplices and they made another appointment to go and rob them again. Unexpectedly, on the second day after the incident, a cousin came to visit the sisters at home and told them about the whole story of repelling the thieves. He knew that the thieves would come back and that there was a spare pistol in this house. He quickly went home to get the gun and carefully instructed the sisters on how to fire it and how to be careful. Two days later, the thieves really came again. The elder sister saw the thieves coming and quickly fired the pistol at them. One thief was immediately hit and fell to the ground and died. The other thieves were shocked, because all of them were empty-handed and had no firearms. They immediately fled and had a big argument with the seamstress. In the end, the police found out about it, arrested them and put them in jail, and severely punished them.

Inscriptions for the Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage Tour

— Zhao Dingming

The Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage Tour took a boat to Xiamen yesterday. A few days ago, the tour leaders, Master Cibei and Master Bi Guan, held a roll of plain silk and went to the Oriental Bookstore Publishing House to ask the editors to write inscriptions. After looking through them, they were all famous calligraphies or poems or insightful essays by famous people at home and abroad. Each was extremely wonderful. I will record them with my pen and share them with the readers.

Our path is not lonely (Yousheng Pilgrimage Tour). Difficult to walk, but able to walk (Wang Zhen). Travel to the Buddhist countries (Xie Weiyin). Buddhist world (Lang Jingshan). Save all living beings (Yan Duhe). The earth is bright (Li Haoran). Coming from thousands of mountains and rivers (Hu Boxiang). Save all living beings from thousands of miles away (Sun Wu). Able to do very difficult and rare things (Yu Youren). Confining the world and suppressing mountains and rivers (Ye Gongchuo). Travel thousands of miles to promote Buddhism (Zhuang Xiquan). Ten years of facing the wall are not as good as traveling thousands of miles (Zhou Shoujuan). Follow in the footsteps of Xuanzang's legacy, and do not let the predecessors be beautiful alone (Huang Jingwan). It is not easy to enter the treasure mountain. Do not let your hands return empty again (Ding Fubao). Activity has wisdom. Wise activity can pacify the world (Yang Yuzhen). A true monk must be able to make Buddhism scientific and Buddhist disciples professional (Lin Jing). Since Bodhidharma came from the west, he was only looking for someone who would not be confused by others (Hu Shi). Go to India to collect the true Dharma of Buddhism and bring it back to China to save the people from fire and water (Gu Qizhong). Traveling in all directions to gain great freedom, and being alone with the spirit of heaven and earth, their aspiration is enough to hold mountains and surpass the sea (Liu Chaoxu). Sending guests away as guests to a far country in the south, I hope that the masters will work hard to make the real world the paradise in our ideals (Wei Juezhong). The true spirit of Buddhism is to benefit the group in almsgiving, precepts, and patience, to cultivate oneself in samadhi and prajna, and to persevere in diligence. One must be able to endure hardship and work hard to go to it. I hope you will encourage each other (Taixu). The Buddhism of China has Mahayana but no Hinayana. Wisdom and faith have high notes, but the precepts are not as good as those of the Hinayana people. I sincerely hope that you will strictly observe the Lengjia meat-eating precepts to be the best. Now that you are traveling in Ceylon, I hope to prove it with this (Zhang Binglin). Sakyamuni Buddha was born more than 2,000 years ago, and his Dharma will spread throughout the world. It is a pity that it has gradually declined since the Qing Dynasty. Now there are Cibei and Biguan comrades who are carrying out the mission of the Buddha and continuing the great aspirations of Faxian and Xuanzang. They have organized a Buddhist pilgrimage tour to explore the relics of the Buddha and his great Dharma and reveal them to the people of the world in order to explain the spirit of the Buddha's compassion and fearlessness. Now, he is about to leave the country. I will record a few words in advance to wish him success (Daxing Zhifeng). (1) I have not participated in Chan in Putuo twice, but I have indulged in idle talk for a hundred years. Life and death depend entirely on your thoughts. How many people worship Buddha to purify their hearts? (2) The Buddha's sitting in the rain is rumored in vain, and the bells and fish are listened to day and night. It is more difficult to distinguish between the threads of the outside world. I recall calling for tea in the library (3) I have rarely experienced hardships, and my waist and feet are still stubborn today. After stepping through a thousand steps of flying sand, I watched the sunrise at the Chaoyang Cave (4) The skirts are carefree, connecting the sea and the sky, and the heroic spirit is returned to the poems. Heaven reserves talent, and there are always a few young years in the eyes (Huang Yanpei). In the eighth century, there was a Jagat Guru in India who came out to promote restorationism in order to exclude Buddhism. In the twelfth century, Islam invaded again, and Buddhism suffered repeated blows and almost disappeared in India. However, the north and south sides have developed in particular. The northward advance was transmitted to the Western Regions and even to China, Korea, and Japan, most of which belonged to Mahayana Buddhism. The southward advance was transmitted to Ceylon, Burma, Siam, Java, and Annam, most of which belonged to Hinayana Buddhism. For thousands of years, they have never been in conflict with each other. Now the Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage Tour does not hesitate to risk the distance to personally visit the countries with India as the end point. Can its thread connect the posts of the north and the south and be a pioneer for the revival of Buddhism? (Jiang Zhuzhuang)

Lotus Root Musings

— Zheng Yimei

A young master chills it with ice, a fair lady relishes it like snow – lotus root! As a thing, it is intricately porous, with fibers deeply intertwined. The ancients called it a "spiritual root emerging from water," and with good reason.

Lotus root can be categorized as field lotus or pond lotus, with pond lotus from southern Jiangsu being of the highest quality. During the late Qing Dynasty, it was often presented as tribute. There is what is called "damaged lotus root," where the leaves taste sweet due to insect damage. Also, the lotus marshes north of Mei Village are famous for producing lotus root; its sweetness and tenderness are not inferior to that of Gaoyou Chefang lotus root, which is incredibly crisp. However, the skin is rough and unsightly, which detracts from its appearance. Judging by appearances to lose out on talented individuals is not limited to lotus root. A single-section lotus root is considered the best, followed by a double-section, and then a triple-section. Triangular lotus roots have small holes and thick flesh, while cylindrical ones have large holes and thin flesh. Anyone purchasing lotus root sections should be aware of this.

Grate fresh lotus root into strands, strain the juice through coarse cloth. After the starch settles, mix it with powdered sugar and then steep it in boiling water. The refreshing fragrance and flavor are a thousand times better than the West Lake white lotus root flour sold in the market. Alternatively, lotus root slices can be mixed with flour and fried in oil, creating what is called lotus root cakes.

To store lotus root, it must be buried in a shady, damp place or wrapped in mud, which allows it to be preserved for a long time.

Some lotus roots have strange and valuable names, such as the dry lotus root of Zhongnan Mountain, mentioned in the Book of Tang; the thousand-often-seen blue lotus root, mentioned in Records of Gleanings; and the jade well lotus flower blooming on the peak of Mount Hua, with ten-foot-long lotus roots like boats, mentioned in Han Yu's "Ancient Meaning." Also, the north produces a three-hole lotus root called "save-trouble-three," all found in Records of Unusual Things.

To represent affection that has not ended, people often use the image of lotus root with connected silk threads. Xia Yizi, a talented man from Shanghai, once used lotus root silk as ink paste. A small jar of ink paste consumed tens, even hundreds, of pounds of lotus root, a rare tale in the artistic world.

Take lotus root nodes, dry them under the eaves for a year, and then use them to brew soup for drinking. It can relieve chest tightness and congestion.

Stuff lotus root holes with glutinous rice and steam it for cooked lotus root, or cook it with porridge for lotus root porridge, truly a refined dish for the home kitchen.

Yang Guifei wore mandarin duck side-by-side lotus patterned brocade trousers and socks. Emperor Xuanzong teased her, saying, "The trousers and socks of the esteemed consort truly have mandarin ducks and lotus flowers! Otherwise, how could there be such white lotus roots inside?" Therefore, Guifei named the trousers and socks "lotus root revival." This magnificence of lotus root is recorded here to complete the lotus root musings.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (51)

— Linghua

Mr. Dai and I discussed the similarities and differences between world ethnic cultures, based on my book "Case Studies in the Eastern University," in which I used evidence from Western scholars, from Heraclitus to modern times, to demonstrate the six major cultural systems of the East: Confucianism, Laoism, Yangism, Mohism, Buddhism, and Taoism. Mr. Wu Zhihui praised it as an unprecedented and unsurpassed work. Among them, Yang's teachings had long been forgotten. I brought them up incidentally and compared them with Heraclitus, connecting them to Bentham's utilitarianism. Yang's teachings are similar to Heraclitus's Epicurean School, which says that "pleasure is the highest good." "Let us eat and drink today, for tomorrow we may not be able to rely on anything." This is no different from Liu Ling and Ji Kang's philosophy of reaching life's limits, or the idea of "bury me when I die; I have wine today, so I'll be drunk today." Mohism, on the other hand, is harsh and demanding, no different from the Judaized Jesus. Yang is close to Heraclitus's pleasure-seeking, while Mo is close to the Jewish asceticism. Lao is close to the naturalness of India, and the Indian philosophy is high and far away, difficult to reach from this lower earth. Confucius's doctrine of the mean is very similar to the golden mean of the three Greek philosophers including Aristotle. Qu Yuan's theory of good governance (see "Universal Peace") is very similar to William Morris's good social policy and today's American social organization law, all of which are the essence of world civilization.

On the 17th, Ms. Li Yunde, the principal of a Fujian girls' school, hosted a banquet at the Kek Lok Si Temple, the most famous scenic spot in Southeast Asia. Clear springs flow from the top of the mountain, and pools are set up along the mountainside to raise flowers, turtles, and fish. The lighting is well-equipped.

On the 18th, I visited the Nanjing Hotel by the sea. The layout is very exquisite. Watching the sea water hit the shore and the tall trees lining the beach. The tall trees here are very similar to those in Beijing parks, except they are not pine trees. Each foreign house hangs a large red lantern, similar to those used in Chinese government offices, with the owner's surname written in large Song Dynasty characters, which is a northern custom. Each household also writes their clan name at the entrance, such as Pengcheng, Tianshui, Xihe, and Anding, to show their clan. It can be seen that the emphasis on surnames is well-developed among overseas Chinese. The houses are all magnificent. In Singapore, many are the color of rice flour, but here the color is slightly lighter because it is close to India. The clothing is mostly yellow, as yellow is considered noble. The monks' robes are also yellow. The betel nut horns in Penang are more beautiful than in other places, and the quality is also firm. The horns are especially long. The rickshaws are larger than those in Singapore, and the trams run too slowly, almost allowing one to get on and off at any place. The skin of the local men and women is still black, but the women are physically very strong, truly slender and graceful, unlike the weakness of our women. Their gait is upright, without any slanting or twisting. But their skin is only black, and their bone structure is still similar to that of Europeans, probably because they are mostly of the Aryan race.

Warmth in the Heart (278)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Green Bamboo Tears, Lady's Heart Broken; Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, Maiden's Soul Departs

Zhang Yiqing rented a two-story house to hide his mistress. At that time, a two-story house in Shanghai only rented for fifteen or sixteen yuan, but he spent several hundred yuan on decoration, wallpapering, and installing electric lights, really bustling for a while. In addition, he bought rosewood foreign furniture, copper beds, mirrors, and screens, everything complete. Cuiyun was also happy and content, thinking she had found her right place. Who knew that in just a few days, she would discover that he had another old woman in Shanghai. Originally, the day he married Cuiyun was the day the Yangtze River steamer departed. His family thought Zhang Yiqing had boarded the ship to Hankou. However, the Yangtze River steamer, after going upstream, always had to go downstream. At most, it would only be seven or eight days before it returned. When it returned, he inevitably had to go home. So, five or six days into the week, Zhang Yiqing explained to her that he had wanted this for a while, it had been done. It was like something he wanted in his heart that he had already gotten his hands on. There was nothing serious about it. He told her, "This woman is not my official wife, but she helped me a lot in the beginning. Now she is old, but I cannot abandon her just because she is old. Of course, I have to appease her, but I really like you, so don't worry." Cuiyun was naturally unhappy. She had clearly been tricked by him, clearly deceived by him. She said, "Then why didn't you explain it clearly in the beginning?" Zhang Yiqing gave a sly smile and said, "If I had explained it clearly, would you still have married me?" Cuiyun's face turned pale upon hearing this. Zhang Yiqing then said, "But please forgive me. The woman in my Ningbo hometown is an ugly villager. She won't come to Shanghai. I won't let her come to Shanghai either. But in my twenty years of doing business in Shanghai, would I never have a woman, always be single? If you think about it, a woman always wants to have a man when she turns twenty. She can't be an old maid forever. Men are the same. You can understand this." Cuiyun thought about it, and it was true. Why hadn't she thought of it in the beginning? But what could she do now? The die was cast. Could she break up with him because of this? Originally, Zhang Yiqing had only spent a little over two thousand yuan to marry Cuiyun. Cuiyun had used the two thousand yuan to pay off her debts and give her father a few hundred yuan. She had also bought some favorite ornaments. The two thousand yuan was long gone. However, Zhang Yiqing, being a famous businessman, had commercial means. He forced Cuiyun's father to write a bill of sale, selling Cuiyun's body to Zhang Yiqing. Zhang Yiqing had obtained all of Cuiyun's rights.

Also, the Osaka spot yarn prices are telegraphed as follows: 20-count Blue Fish is 139 yuan, unchanged, equivalent to 173.8 taels of Shanghai standard; 20-count Red God of Wealth is 135 yuan, unchanged, equivalent to 168.8 taels of Shanghai standard; 16-count Fukushima is 138 yuan, up 3 yuan, equivalent to 172.5 taels of Shanghai standard; 16-count Three Horses is 138 yuan, up 3 yuan, equivalent to 172.5 taels of Shanghai standard.

Grains: Hexia Rice Market is Flat

Zhabei: Yesterday, the supply from Lilu was very scarce, and sales were flat. Broken indica rice reached over 100 shi, with prices opening at 20 yuan and 7.5 jiao. The situation appeared hidden. There was not much high-quality West Xinjing rice, with a total of about 200 shi. The price was 20 yuan and 5 jiao. Dong Xinjing rice initially showed a softening trend, but due to the weather turning cloudy again, it temporarily maintained the original market. The price was still 20 yuan. The overall indica rice situation was very flat. The demand for new Yangjian rice was average, and the supply was also scarce. Prices opened at 14 yuan and 7-8 jiao. New Kejian rice arrived in abundance, and the outflow was not smooth. The general price was 13 yuan and 5-6 jiao. The sales of Baiyuan rice were not good, and the price opened at 18 yuan and 8 jiao.

South Shanghai: The arrival of river rice was declining, and sales were not smooth. The Changbang white indica rice was extremely scarce. The top-quality of Lin Tong's broken indica rice opened at 19 yuan and 5 jiao, and the overall trend was stable. New indica rice has turned to sideways movement, so the price seemed to fluctuate slightly. The arrival and sales of Southbang thin early rice were both sluggish, and market transactions were very limited. The supply of Yangjian rice was continuous, and the sales of new Jian rice were still brisk. The above overall prices were generally unchanged. The top-quality rice opened at 14 yuan at Guanzuo.

Early Machine Rice Arrives in Abundance, Price Drops

Yesterday, customer indica rice continued to arrive, with machine early indica rice accounting for the majority. The local market had a slightly weaker appetite, and the customer merchants' intentions were even more stagnant. The entire market only saw Yantai merchants buying 200 bags of Hunan broken rice. Other merchants did not inquire. Therefore, the market sentiment turned soft. Machine early indica rice had a relatively large inventory, and the price fell slightly. Other types of rice remained stable. The total sales for the day included 400 bags of Hunan Jing rice, 1,000 bags of Jiangxi machine early indica rice, 300 bags of machine late indica rice, and 300 bags of machine yuan rice. Except for the 200 bags of Xiang rice loaded by Yantai, all were purchased by local merchants.

30,000 Bags of Foreign Rice Still Exist

The foreign rice floating in the market has long been sold out. The amount purchased and stored by hoarders and rice shops is also small. Most of it is distributed to customers or sold retail. Therefore, there has long been no price quotation for foreign rice in the South Market and the General Association. According to a survey of the rice industry, the total amount of foreign rice stored in Shanghai, excluding rice shops and odd quantities, is still about 30,000 bags of Xiaojiao rice and several thousand bags of other types of rice. This batch of goods is prepared for sale at flat prices. Currently, new rice has entered the market, and rice prices are gradually falling. The authorities believe that there is no need to engage in flat price sales in the future. Therefore, the 30,000 bags of Xiaojiao rice in storage are planned to be sold in the market in the coming days.

Wheat Futures Rebound Due to Short Covering

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed an upward trend in the morning and afternoon. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat was only about 0.2 yuan lower, the sentiment was naturally soft in the initial session. However, short sellers who had profited were taking this opportunity, believing that time should not be lost, and covered their positions on a large scale. Therefore, the sluggish situation suddenly turned lively. It is speculated that the psychology of covering short positions is due to the fact that although foreign wheat is cost-effective, it still requires a 5.1 tael opening fee. According to the standard, it still exceeds quite a bit. Therefore, they are taking the opportunity to cover their positions, or they may have to re-enter the market in the future. It seems that the current situation is still under the control of short sellers. As a result, the current month rose 4 cents compared to the previous day, October rose 4 cents, November rose 5 cents, December rose 7 cents, and January and February rose 6 cents. The spot wheat market remains sluggish, but manufacturers see that the market price is already low and have started to act. Secondary goods have fallen about 0.1 yuan compared to the previous week, and nearly 0.2 yuan compared to the beginning of this month. The entire market opened with over 9,000 bags of wheat from Taierzhuang, Yaowan, and Haizhou. About 6,000 bags were purchased by factories such as Fufeng and Shenda.

Flour Market Still Difficult to be Optimistic

Yesterday, the flour market trended sideways in the morning and afternoon. Since the quoted price of foreign wheat was cut by another 0.2 yuan, the sentiment in the initial opening was not great. Distant months were about 0.1 yuan softer than the closing price of the previous day. Then, due to the strong short covering from various firms and factories, prices rebounded. By the time the afternoon session opened, because futures prices rebounded due to short covering... (the sentence is cut off mid-way).

The buying interest from both domestic and foreign sources also turned slightly lively. However, the environment is no longer what it used to be. Customers have foreign flour in preparation, and factories have already started ordering foreign wheat. Therefore, if the ban on sales to the north is lifted and flour has a way out, the market may turn stable. Otherwise, the selling pressure is strong and it is not easy to be optimistic. As a result, the current month was down 0.25%, October was down 0.5%, November was down 0.25%, December was up 0.25%, January was up 0.5%, and February was unchanged.

Textiles: Eastern Goods Turn Downward Quickly

The rising trend in the Eastern goods textile market has ceased recently, and yesterday it even turned downward quickly. This is because the price increase last week was too severe, resulting in sluggish real sales. Holders of goods found it difficult to sell them off in the short term, causing the market sentiment to soften sharply. Yesterday, Yuehua velvet was down 0.25%, and Wakayama's Three Children black flower was selling at 1.9 yuan per share. Most medium-sized handles were selling at 1.95 yuan. Last week, Jiangsu merchants had offered 2 yuan and 0.2%, a drop of 7.5%. Gongduan Gongni was uniformly down 0.25%, and cotton flannel was also down slightly. Yesterday, Fuhua's large group was 1.875 yuan, and the concubine color was 1.775 yuan. Only bleached cloth remained firm. The Magpie Bridge Meeting opened at 10.08 taels, Shuang Zongtong at 10.085 taels, Guo Ziyi at 10.075 taels, and Flower Bird at 7.75 taels. Foreign standard Chongsu silk, Gaitaorong, and others did not have significant changes. Customer sales were very quiet. The Tianjin merchants, who had been active for a while, have now stopped operating. The Yangtze River basin remains stagnant. Local merchants are even more reluctant to take delivery of goods. Only Sichuan merchants are slightly active.

Northern and Southern Goods: Xiang Lian Arrives Scarcely, Price Rises

This year's Xiang Lian production was abundant, but the arrival of goods has been scarce recently, causing prices to rise steadily. This is because the current situation is that local areas are suffering from frequent disturbances, and cash is often plundered. Owners of goods consider hiding money as a dangerous pursuit and turn to hiding goods instead. Therefore, the arrival of goods is scarce. Currently, the prices in the Shanghai market are: Xiangtan lotus seeds at 45 taels, Raozhou lotus seeds at 44 taels, Hengzhou lotus seeds at 44 taels, Changde lotus seeds at 42 taels, and white lotus seeds at 42 taels. The market sentiment is stable.

Local News

This Year's Plague and Rat Plague

Dr. Wu Lien-teh's Investigation Report

The investigation report by Dr. Wu Lien-teh, Director of the National Epidemic Prevention Bureau and concurrently Director of the Northeast Provinces Epidemic Prevention Bureau, on plague and other epidemics in China has been published. The main contents are as follows: (1) Plague: In the summer of last year, Liu Ruiheng, Minister of Health, repeatedly convened Shanghai health experts to discuss measures to prevent and control plague. Dr. Qiao Teng, Director of the Health Department of the Shanghai Public Concession Board, Mr. Fantia of the French Concession Board, and Dr. Hu Hongji, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Government Health Bureau, were all present. It was decided to establish a

Central Plague Bureau to collect reports on plague epidemics from various locations and distribute them to relevant agencies for reference. At that time, Dr. Wu was appointed as the director to oversee everything. The bureau was attached to the Epidemic Prevention Bureau. In order to investigate the medium of plague transmission and trace the origin of the epidemic, Dr. Wu transferred several specialists from his Harbin office to Shanghai to carry out this work. All research procedures were conducted in the sanitary laboratory set up by the government. (Note: The bureau also has many experts specializing in the study of the occurrence of germs and the injection to resist plague.) This work began on June 1 of this year and continued until August 28, totaling three months. A total of 1,600 stool samples from patients with various intestinal and abdominal diseases were collected from various locations in Shanghai. Although microorganisms resembling plague were found in more than 50 of these 1,600 samples, the true source of plague (Vibrio) that is believed by doctors was not found at all. It was not until August 28 that a true case of plague occurred in a person in Hongkou Hospital. The patient recovered soon after treatment in the hospital. According to investigations, a total of 49 cases of this disease were successively infected from that time until September, and only four people died as a result. The rest all recovered after treatment. Several points are noteworthy about the outbreak of plague this time: (1) The disease is not very dangerous; (2) It began to occur after the hot weather had passed; (3) It began to occur long after the watermelon season; (4) The epidemic will probably not last long. At present, Shanghai health authorities are making every effort to cooperate in seeking ways to curb it. It is still difficult to predict the effect of the municipal government's anti-epidemic injections. The 600,000 doses of injections that have been used are all manufactured by domestic laboratories. By the end of August, the Public Concession had administered 66,338 doses of injections. By September 14, the French Concession had administered a total of 66,021 doses. By the end of August, the Municipal Government Health Department had administered a total of 377,212 doses. (2) Other Epidemics: The Northeast Provinces Epidemic Prevention Bureau must prevent the occurrence of rat plague in the southern Manchuria regions bordering Mongolia every year. In mid-August, a Chinese worker in a village in Mongolia suddenly developed this disease. By August 14, a total of 30 cases of rat plague had been recorded. At the beginning of this month, Wang Yicun, a medical officer sent by Harbin to investigate epidemics, discovered that there was a rat plague epidemic among the cavalry stationed in Tongliao. Every day, four or five people died from this epidemic. In addition, there were four cases of rat plague in a village near the Kaitong Railway, but the investigation was extremely difficult due to the heavy floods in the area. Approximately 60 cases of rat plague will occur this year. There is no doubt that the nature of this rat plague is true rat plague. These several locations are the source of the rat plague, and multiple cases must occur every year. It is deeply hoped that the Epidemic Prevention Bureau will do its best to prevent it from being easily eliminated. The recent news of a rat plague epidemic issued by the Japanese News Agency is not overly alarming. As soon as the Northeast Provinces Epidemic Prevention Bureau hears of an epidemic in a certain place, it immediately sends medical officers to curb it and will never let it spread.

Latest News on Shanghai-Chongqing Aviation

Jiujiang Returns to Shanghai Yesterday

Hoping to Re-Fly in the Coming Days

The setback in the Shanghai-Chongqing line test flight of the China National Aviation Corporation has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the Jiujiang aircraft flew back to Shanghai at 4 pm yesterday, waiting for the Ministry of Transport to negotiate with Liu Xiang before re-flying. After the setback occurred, He Yingqin, Commander-in-Chief of Hankou, and Wang Boqun, Minister of Transport, sent telegrams to Sichuan Liu respectively. Yesterday, a reply telegram was received from Commander Liu, hoping that the Ministry of Transport would send someone to Chongqing to discuss the matter in person. However, the Ministry of Transport believed that sending someone would take a long time, so it immediately sent a long telegram detailing everything. A decision will be made after receiving a reply telegram. However, the airline hopes to re-fly in the coming days, otherwise the originally scheduled official flight of Shanghai-Chongqing aviation in early October will be difficult and will therefore be suspended. Smith, the head of the air navigation team, Hamilton, the vice chairman, and Bian Fugeng, a mechanic, arrived in Shanghai with the plane yesterday. Nie Kaiyi, the deputy director, deplaned in Beijing and did not come.

Issue of Japanese Cocoons Imported into China

Customs Strictly Prohibits Importation: This port's customs authorities yesterday received an instruction from the Ministry of Finance, stating that in order to comply with the case, Administrative Yuan Instruction No. 3241 was followed. The instruction stated that a letter from the Civilian Affairs Office of the National Government, forwarded by the Chairman, mentioned a telegram from the Jiaxing County Merchants' United Committee, stating that the import of Japanese cocoons into Shanghai harmed domestic production, and the actions of treacherous merchants buying them were outrageous. It was heard that several batches were waiting to be imported. If this was not quickly prohibited, the consequences would be unthinkable. It was requested that the customs authorities be ordered to strictly prohibit the import of all Japanese cocoons to prevent future troubles and protect domestic production. The Chairman ordered an investigation and handed the case to the Executive Yuan for investigation and handling. It was noted that the Central Executive Committee's Secretariat had previously received a telegram from Zhejiang cocoon merchants Jiang Shifang and others, stating that Japanese cocoons were being sold cheaply in China, affecting Chinese cocoons, and requesting heavy taxation. This was approved and handed over to the Executive Yuan for investigation and handling. As the previous reasons were now received again, a corresponding letter was sent to inform them and instructed them to handle the matter accordingly. It was noted that Zhejiang cocoon merchants Jiang Shifang and others had previously submitted a telegram to the Executive Yuan, which was handed over to the Ministry for review. Now, according to the previous instructions, in addition to sending a reply and issuing separate orders, the Ministry should be ordered to quickly instruct the customs authorities to strictly prohibit the import of all Japanese cocoons to protect domestic production. Upon receiving this order, the Customs Superintendent, Hua Jiwen, had already instructed all subordinates to comply.

Reasons Stated by Manufacturers: The General Association of Silk and Cocoons of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui sent a circular, stating that the Jiaxing Cocoon Industry Association, the Haiyan Cocoon Industry Association, the Shengzhu and Xin Three Counties Cocoon Industry Association, and all farmers in Jiahu, including Mr. Jiang Laixian, Zhao Jiexiang, Lu Qianan, Wang Weisan, Cheng Huilian, Zhong Bosen, and the Hai'ning Cocoon Industry, including Zhong Guangyan and Wang Qingquan, all noted that they had received letters and telegrams regarding the issue of Japanese cocoons being imported and suppressing cocoons, harming cocoon merchants and farmers. They were fully aware of the concerns of the public and the protection of farmers and merchants, and admired them beyond words. However, the situation in this case may not be fully understood by the public, leading to misunderstandings. The facts must be explained in detail to dispel rumors. This year's cocoon harvest is poor, and the situation in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is roughly the same. The Zhejiang factories are slightly less affected, only about one-sixth of the production of Jiangsu Province, and may be able to barely maintain the status quo. However, if Jiangsu is considered, there are about 150 factories in Shanghai and Wuxi, with approximately 38,000 machines. The amount of dried cocoon raw materials needed for the entire year of twelve months is about 500,000 dan. It was previously investigated that the cocoon production in Jiangsu and the amount transported from other provinces, as well as a small number of summer cocoons, was less than 300,000 dan. The supply and demand are barely balanced, with a shortage of about 45%. If there is no relief measure, the factories will have to stop reeling after only six or seven months of work. How can the livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of male and female workers in the factories not be pitied? This is why it is necessary to plan for the mulberry land and barely continue the work. This is the reason for purchasing Japanese cocoons. This matter was discussed in June, and most of the colleagues in the Shanghai factories requested the Industry Association to find a solution. The association then submitted a petition, specifically to avoid import duties, as the purchase of foreign cocoons is subject to tariffs and is not prohibited. Moreover, this is a temporary relief measure of a limited nature, so there is no need to apply for registration. The Ministry approved a reduction in tariffs, taxing 7.5% of the value, limited to 60,000 dan, until March of next year, and other industries may not follow suit. This is the fact of purchasing Japanese cocoons. The General Association planned this temporary relief measure entirely for the future of silk merchants and factory workers, without any bias. In this era of cocoon shortage, the import of 60,000 dan of Japanese cocoons is to alleviate the cocoon shortage, and there is still concern that it may not be enough. How can it suppress Chinese cocoons and invade the farmers? Moreover, the restrictions are strict and under our control, so there will be no other abuses. Unexpectedly, letters and telegrams flew in, saying that it was collusion, Japanese invasion, and Japanese sabotage. Who is not a colleague? Who is a treacherous merchant? The accusations were deafening. But who knew why? It has been observed that when there is a shortage of rice in the inland, Saigon rice is purchased to feed the people. When yarn factories lack raw materials, foreign cotton is purchased. When flour mills lack wheat, American wheat is purchased to maintain work. Farmers and merchants have never been heard to call for obstructing Chinese rice, invading Chinese cotton, or sabotaging Chinese wheat. For years, Japanese merchants have purchased double-cocoon goods for export, with raw materials flowing out. We have only heard requests from manufacturers to ban them, and have not heard a single word from cocoon merchants. Promoting the collection of raw materials and the export of products is essential for the industrial world in the East and West, and is not comparable to the import of finished goods solely to invade the economy. There is a clear distinction between these positive and negative proportions, and accusations should not be made based on common rhetoric. Currently, Japanese cocoons have not yet arrived in China, but the purchase of cocoons is limited and the demand for cocoons is still greater than this number. Even if 60,000 dan are purchased, it is still hoped that the remaining cocoons can be sold by merchants. Farmers have already become indirectly harmless. Even if cocoon merchants hold cocoons and seek to sell them at higher prices, it will not hinder their interests. Planning with chopsticks, there is no need to worry unnecessarily and make a fuss over nothing. If the cocoon market next year is a concern, the restrictions are in place before the new cocoons come out, and no cocoons beyond the 60,000 dan will be imported, so there is no concern about the destruction of cocoons and mulberry or the devouring of manufacturers. Otherwise, how could the ruling officials not know the disadvantages and approve it so quickly, as the public said? What the public said is mostly for the cocoon industry, but the position of the General Association has to take into account both the factory and the industry, adjusting the surplus and reducing the shortage. It is important to be expedient, using Chu talents for the purpose of relief. The public is clear and should be able to understand. Recently, newspapers have been spreading rumors that Japanese cocoons are coming to China, and that the transport of cocoons has been suspended. We cannot determine the truth or falsehood, but the autumn cocoon harvest has also been poor, and cannot make up for the loss of the spring cocoons. The actual need is that the purchase of Japanese cocoons must be carried out according to the plan. We hope that you will be calm and patient, and we will never let the remaining cocoons of Chinese merchants have the worry of being stored and tragically dropped. We sincerely reply, hoping to dispel misunderstandings and hoping for understanding.

Two Organizations Oppose Increasing Water Prices

City Chamber of Commerce Issues Declaration of Opposition

Taxpayers' Association Requests Withdrawal of Price Increase Proposal

The case of the public concession increasing water prices has aroused opposition from various organizations. Yesterday, the City Chamber of Commerce also issued a declaration of opposition, and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a long letter to the Public Works Department, based on the facts, requesting the withdrawal of the price increase proposal to comply with public opinion. The original letter is recorded below.

City Chamber of Commerce Issues Declaration: The City Chamber of Commerce issued a declaration stating that the Public Concession Water Company, using the excuse of a sharp decline in the exchange rate, requested an increase in water prices by 25%, which was passed by the Public Works Department's Board of Directors. All sectors of the city, as well as various agencies and organizations, believe that this move violates public interest and disregards the interests of the people, and have raised protests, pointing out the reasons in great detail. The association has two more opinions to which it respectfully requests the attention of all sectors: (1) Regarding the water price fixed rate period, the contract signed between the company and the Public Works Department stipulated a period of five years. In terms of the principle of the sanctity of contracts, the company cannot violate the rules and request a price increase within the stipulated period of the contract, and the Public Works Department cannot violate the rules and approve a price increase. The company argues that the exchange rate has plummeted and the annual dividend is not enough to cover the costs. Is this reason enough to suddenly allow a price increase before the expiration of the period? Does the original contract have such an exception? We should ask the Public Works Department to publicly review the contract. Otherwise, the Public Works Department should be responsible for disregarding the interests of all citizens by allowing a price increase before the contract expires. (2) Should this kind of direct increase in the burden on citizens be decided by the citizens themselves, or can it be entrusted to the City Board of Directors to decide on their behalf? After this lesson, we should feel that the city system in the concession needs fundamental revision. At the very least, we should strive for Chinese taxpayers to participate in the taxpayers' annual meeting on an equal footing with foreigners residing in Shanghai, so that the entire opinion of the citizens can be raised to make a powerful decision on issues related to the interests of the citizens themselves. As the saying goes, scholars must be ambitious and have a long way to go. May all citizens have keen eyes and meticulous steps to move forward.

Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to Public Works Department: The Taxpayers' Association yesterday sent a letter to the Board of Directors of the Public Concession Public Works Department, stating that the General Assembly of the association had previously discussed the case of increasing water prices in the Public Concession on September 5 and decided that the case was related to increasing the burden on residents and needed to be carefully reconsidered. In addition to handing it over to the Executive Committee to form a special committee for careful study, the Public Works Department should first be informed by letter to suspend the implementation of the price increase proposal. The association had previously recorded the case on September 6 and sent a special letter to your bureau to take note of it. Now, after the special committee for this case has studied the results, it believes that the price increase of public concession water should be prevented in terms of law and reason. The industry specifically requests your bureau to follow the public opinion of the residents and immediately withdraw the original proposal. The reasons for the withdrawal are described below: (A) In terms of legal theory, according to the contract signed between the Public Concession Public Works Department and the Shanghai Water Company on March 17, 1928, the effective period is 20 years. During the effective period of the contract, the Public Works Department has no need to consider any request made by the Water Company that violates the contract in terms of legal theory or approval. Moreover, according to Article 13 of the contract, the water price period must be five years, and the Public Works Department's announcement in 1929 changed it to two years. The Public Works Department cannot but bear the responsibility for this disregard for the sanctity of the contract. Even if it is said that it can be modified with the consent of both parties, this is a public utility, and every move is related to the third party of residents, and it is not a purely contractual relationship that stipulates the rights and obligations of the two parties. Taking a step back, even if the water price period has been changed to two years, it must be changed until July 1, 1931, and a proposal must be made five months before the deadline. Now, the deadline has not arrived, and the procedures are lacking. How can the Public Works Department immediately approve the company's request and rashly consider it or approve it? In terms of legal theory, the Public Works Department's approval of the company's price increase is fundamentally invalid. (B) In terms of fact (1) The Water Company's proposed price increase is due to the sharp decline in the British-Shanghai exchange rate and the rise in prices. As a result, this year's net profit is not enough to cover the annual dividend. However, the sharp decline in the exchange rate is a temporary phenomenon. For example, the British exchange rate at the time the Water Company proposed the price increase was 1 shilling and 6 pence, according to the announcement on August 6. But the current British exchange rate has changed to 1 shilling and 7 pence and 25 pence. Compared to the two, the exchange rate has gradually increased. The Water Company cannot base its future speculation on a temporary phenomenon. The first reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of the exchange rate. (2) The company said that the price of goods has risen, and the water fee should be raised accordingly. However, the payment of water fees is calculated based on the rent, not independently. In other words, according to the rent percentage of six, Shanghai rents have increased year by year due to the prosperity of the population and the shortage of supply. Since the water price is calculated with the rent, it will naturally continue to increase every year. For example, the rent 25 years ago was only 50 yuan per month in the same location, but now it requires 300 yuan, which is an eightfold increase compared to before. The water price also increases by eightfold accordingly. The second reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of the high rent. (3) The company said that the dividend is not enough to reach the maximum limit of 9%, which will not attract new capital and lead to the stagnation of business. However, the association believes that this reason is not sufficient. For example, the sale of the electrical station has 8.1 million taels of silver, and recently the Shanghai Electric Power Company issued 2 million taels of 6% preferred shares, which were immediately gathered. Also, when the China and Foreign Telephone Company tendered, there were as many as three companies competing to purchase it. This is also enough to prove the ease of gathering capital. Moreover, there is a risk of bad debts and rotten debts in the electricity and telephone business, and they are not necessities that individuals must use. As for tap water, on the one hand, it is necessary for residents to use, and on the other hand, the landlord remits the water price, without the labor of collecting it from each household. It is the most stable and reliable business in public utilities. How can there be such a stable and reliable business that is not enough to attract capital? The third reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of fundraising. (4) The company must increase prices due to insufficient dividend payments. I do not know to what extent the company's so-called insufficient refers to. If it is said that it is not enough to pay 9%, then the contract must stipulate that the dividend

Page 14

9% must not be exceeded or reduced. However, the contract only stipulates that the dividend is up to 9%. It can be known that the dividend can be paid at any rate below 9%. Since the company has no basis to pay 9%, the Public Works Department has no reason to order residents to pay the company's shareholders at the highest interest rate. Moreover, even if the company's dividend must be paid at 9%, it can be supplemented by future profits according to the contract. If it is said that the exchange rate will definitely not rise and there is no hope, then the London price of silver in 1920 rose to 61.5 pence, and the Shanghai exchange rate rose to 8 or 9 shillings. I am afraid that no one could have predicted it before the deadline. The company benefited greatly from the pound at that time. Why did it not propose to reduce the price? It did not reduce the price when the British exchange rate was high, but it requested a price increase when the British exchange rate was short. Judging from the circumstances, is it peaceful? The fourth reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of dividends. (5) The company recently published a talk in the Mainland News, saying that the number of water users has increased due to the increase in population, believing that it is necessary to increase prices. However, at the same time, the company did not take into account how many more buildings there were than 25 years ago, how much more the total rent was than 25 years ago, and how much the actual price of water per thousand gallons was 25 years ago and how much it is now. If the rate of population increase, the rate of rent increase, and the actual price rate per thousand gallons of package water are made into statistics for detailed examination, then the company's talk will be difficult to make people believe. Perhaps the company knew this statistic clearly, but deliberately did not publish it publicly? The fifth reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of population increase. (6) The company said that the cost of labor and materials is too high, resulting in huge expenses, and the remaining profit is not enough to distribute dividends. However, the water price has increased with the increase of rent, so there is no reason why it is not enough to allocate it. Moreover, due to the increase in the amount of business, according to the principles of industrial economics, its benefits must be increased. According to the survey, the price of tap water in the public concession is 50 cents per thousand gallons, while the price of water in the southern city of Zhabei is only 45 cents per thousand gallons. The same enterprise has the same labor and materials, and the price and business are better than the other. Who can believe that there is no profit? Moreover, the water pipes and installation costs of the branch pipes are borne by the landlord. The company does not bear any of the costs on the water pipes, and can also get a sales profit. Also, the water price should be charged at 6% of the rent, but the actual amount obtained exceeds 6%. For example, if the rent is 100 taels and the water fee is 6 taels, the actual rent is only 94 taels. The water fee of 6 taels is charged on 94 taels, and the income is already 6.39%. This extra income is 0.36 per 100 taels, and the total is also considerable. The sixth reason why the price increase case should not be established in terms of the cost of labor and materials. While the case was being reviewed, it was approved that the City Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Real Estate Association and other groups have sent letters for the same reason, which is enough to prove that opposing the increase in water prices is the public opinion of all residents. A corresponding letter is sent, hoping that your bureau will review it and immediately withdraw the case of approving the Shanghai Water Company's increase in prices by 25%. In order to clarify the company's content to the residents, your bureau should organize a special committee to investigate the company's accounts over the years, prepare a report, and publish it to prevent the company from taking improper profits by using the monopoly of public utilities. We also hope that your bureau will clearly announce the withdrawal of this case and reply. This is addressed to the Board of Directors of the Public Concession Public Works Department.

Record of the Real Estate Association Meeting

Discussing the Water Price Increase Case

The Shanghai Real Estate Association held its second meeting at 4 pm yesterday.
