Explanation from Shanghai Water Company

Reply to the Real Estate Association Letter

The Shanghai Water Company replied to the Shanghai Real Estate Association on the 15th of this month, stating that they had received your letter of September 9 protesting against the company's recent increase in water fees by 25%, which was approved by the Public Works Department and notified to users. The case has been carefully considered by both parties before being approved by the Public Works Department and the company. After reading your letter, the directors of the company respectfully reply to the items stated in your letter as follows: Your association said that the company has not reduced prices when the exchange rate was high. According to the contract signed between the company and the Public Works Department from 1905 to 1927, the water price was fixed and the calculation of dividends was unlimited. Moreover, after the European War, the prices of all goods soared. Although the exchange rate was high at that time, the company did not take much profit. If the contract signed between the company and the Public Works Department cannot be changed according to the times, the company will not be able to attract capital and meet the increasing demand for water. The contract signed between the company and the Public Works Department on March 17, 1928, stated that the company's dividend was fixed and the water price could be revised from time to time. Your association said that the company is making high profits for shareholders with the money of the citizens. The company cannot admit this because the interest rate distributed to each shareholder must not exceed the interest rate approved by the Public Works Department. Your association should be able to understand the above two points, so that users did not enjoy the benefit when the exchange rate was high. If the exchange rate could be high after the company and the Public Works Department signed the contract in 1928, users would be able to enjoy the benefit. Therefore, when the Public Works Department approved the company's price increase, it was attached with the condition that if the price of silver in Shanghai rose to about 2 shillings, the price increase should be reconsidered. Your association suggested that the company use the security deposit stored in the (average share price) and (revised budget) to make up for the deficit. The company is difficult to implement because there is no surplus in the (revised budget). It can be understood after reviewing the recently published accounts. The (average share price) was also considered before the company passed the price increase proposal. The revenue of tap water has increased with the soaring rent in recent years, as your association said. However, since the city adopted the Gregorian calendar, the company no longer has the unexpected income of leap months, and the consumption of users is also increasing day by day. It is expected that this year's consumption will be twice as high as in the past. The raw material of tap water is indeed the water of the Huangpu River. However, it takes a lot of expensive projects and equipment to draw the water, filter it, and make it usable for users. The water of the Huangpu River can be used without spending a penny, but the cost of the drawing projects and equipment is increasing day by day. The directors of the company hope that your association can send several representatives to visit the company's water intake pool in Yangshupu, so that your association may believe that the company's words are true. Although the installation of branch pipes is funded by the owners, the cost of daily maintenance of the pipes is still borne by the company. The contract signed between the company and the Public Works Department in 1928 stated in detail that the water price can be revised at any time (with the consent of both parties). So, how has the company violated the contract? Moreover, the current water price is based on the exchange rate of 2 shillings and 5 pence. Now the exchange rate has suddenly fallen to 1 shilling and 7 pence. How can the company not increase it to maintain the needs of the public in Shanghai? If your association considers this point in detail, it may also recognize that the company's price increase is reasonable. If your association's representatives can take the time to visit the company's Yangshupu factory, the company will sincerely welcome them to explain everything in person. This is addressed to the Shanghai Real Estate Association, Shanghai Water Company Secretary Hua De respectfully replied.

Flour Begins to Be Transported North

Northern Inspection of Merchant Ships

Flour Transported to Tianjin: Since the Shanghai Jianghai Customs prohibited the transport of flour to North China, foreign flour has taken the opportunity to enter. The number of American wheat flour shipped to Beiyang has increased day by day. Flour mills in Shanghai requested the Ministry of Finance to lift the ban on the transport of wheat flour to North China for business reasons, in order to maintain the people's food supply and resist the import of foreign flour. This matter has been discussed for a long time. The Ministry of Finance has now accepted the request of the flour mills and approved the lifting of the ban. The flour mills have publicly recognized the purchase of 1 million in public bonds. Recently, the mills have been in contact with various shipping companies to handle transportation procedures. According to the Shanghai shipping price for wheat flour to Tianjin, it is fixed at 4.2 cents per bag. After the actual receipt of 1.89 cents, foreign merchants competed to drop the price to 9 cents per bag. Due to this rate of loss being too large, the transportation companies have proposed a public discussion and resolved to increase it to 1.1 cents per bag. Yesterday, a British ship in the port began to load flour to Tianjin. This is the first batch after the ban was lifted. In recent days, British and Japanese ships have been competing fiercely to solicit this northward transport of wheat flour.

Inspection of Merchant Ships: There are thirteen regular ships from five companies in Shanghai to Beiyang: Taikoo, Ewo, Nisshin, Osaka Shosen, and Zhaoshang, all of which reach Tianjin Baihe and even Zizhu Lin. Recently, after the defeat of the Northern Army, Tianjin has been very vigilant and pays special attention to ships going south. The Tianjin Customs has recently dispatched inspectors to search merchant ships. When ships from Shanghai to Tianjin sail to Tanggu Port, the inspectors take small boats to Dazhan to wait for the ships. They board the ships to search, especially carefully inspecting passengers traveling south and thoroughly inspecting luggage and items, causing great annoyance to passengers. Recently, British and Japanese ships have raised serious protests, saying that it hinders their business.

Li Was a Confidant of Wang Jingwei

Li was a confidant of Wang Jingwei in Peiping. This time, he was dispatched by Wang to Shanghai to take on some important work. After his travel expenses ran out, he conceived a robbery. Li was the mastermind behind this case. After the robbery, they gathered at Li's residence at No. 66 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession. Li distributed 2,000 yuan to him. The next day, he went to Li's residence again. Li's wife told him that Li had returned to Peiping. He rushed to Fengtian (Mukden) to meet Li and decided to go north together. Li gave him another 220 yuan to buy a boat ticket, telling him not to implicate others and to find a way to rescue him.

When they were about to pass Dagu, Li said that there must be detectives guarding the Dagu port, and he should quickly shave his beard and remove his gold teeth to avoid attracting attention. He had to shave his beard, and Li helped him pull out his teeth, and told him that if he was still caught, don't implicate others, and Li promised to find a way to rescue him. That's why he didn't say Li's real name when he was arrested and said that he had never known him. He was following Li's instructions. Now that Li is with Wang Jingwei in Peiping, he can lead the way to arrest him, etc. The Tianjin police finally realized it, but they had already released him and could not arrest him. The Tianjin local authorities requested extradition.

When we received the warrant from your court and arrived in Tianjin, the Chinese authorities there were negotiating with the Tianjin Municipal Council to request the extradition of Zhu. This must be the result of Li's finding a way to help Zhu after returning to Peiping. If Zhu is handed over to the Chinese officials, he will definitely be released because the Chinese authorities there do not recognize the warrant from your court that we showed them. The Tianjin Municipal Council handed Zhu directly over to us without going through the Chinese territory and directly boarded the ship to escort him back. Along the way, the photos of those related to this case were shown to Zhu. Zhu gave a detailed confession about the process of the case and the degree of involvement of each defendant in the case. Then, the confession was submitted to the court for investigation to determine whether Zhu Desheng was the ringleader of the robbery.

According to the interrogation by Judge Zhou, Zhu the thief confessed that he was in the countryside this year when he was summoned to Shanghai by his friend Gao Guowei, who promised to introduce him to a job. When he arrived in Shanghai, Gao introduced him to Li Zuquan. Li asked him to recruit several guards, so he asked Liang Houbiao to recommend him to Sheng, who recommended Wang E, He Guo, Wang Yang, etc. At first, he didn't know that Li had gathered people to plan the robbery. When the robbery was taking place, he was sitting in a rickshaw watching from a distance. The rest of his confession was similar to what the Western detectives reported, but he denied being the ringleader. Wang E claimed that Zhu was indeed the leader.

During the next interrogation, Wang E confessed that Zhu Desheng was indeed the ringleader. Before the robbery, Zhu asked Liang Houbiao to invite me to a hotel to discuss and decided that Zhu, Wang Yang, He Guo, and the two who are at large, Ma and Su, together with me, would go to rob. Afterwards, we went to a garden on Jin Shenfu Road to divide the loot. I got 1,650 yuan. Wang Yang got the same amount. Sheng Cheng only got 500 yuan as an introduction fee. We only knew that Zhu was the leader, and we didn't know there was a Mr. Li. The rest of the thieves' confessions were very vague.

During another interrogation, He Guo confessed that he was introduced to Zhu by Liang to be a guard. When the robbery took place, Zhu ordered me to go with him and gave me a pistol. At first, I didn't want to go, but Zhu shot at me, and the scar on my face is still there. I had to follow him and listen to his commands. Afterwards, Zhu gave me 1,000 yuan. Wang Yang also confessed that although he was in the same gang as them, he was not at the scene during the robbery. The rest of his words were evasive. In addition, although Liang Houbiao and other male and female defendants were interrogated one by one, their confessions were ambiguous. Wang and Wang were bandits who committed a kidnapping in Jiaxing.

The victim of the robbery, Wang Fuchang, hired a lawyer to represent him and requested a thorough investigation. Huan Guanlin, the chief detective of the Jiaxing County Government, did not appear in court, stating that Wang E and Wang Yang had committed a kidnapping case in Jiaxing, and the ransom was still missing. He requested that the two bandits be temporarily taken back to Jiaxing for one week to investigate the whereabouts of the ransom. The family members of the ransom victim also hired a lawyer to help them request the transfer. Judge Zhou then ordered that Wang E and Wang Yang be temporarily taken away by the Jiaxing Court for investigation and sent back within a week. He Xu Shi was released on bail, and the rest of the male and female defendants were returned to prison to be investigated and interrogated again in fourteen days.

Tangjiawan Fire Tragedy

Pan A’xin’s Carelessness Causes Great Disaster

Chen Guobao’s Whole Family Loses Three Lives

At 10:15 yesterday morning, a sudden fire broke out at No. 71 Tangjiawan Road in the Nanshi area. Four municipal houses were destroyed, two girls and one woman were burned to death, and one boy fell from the building and broke his leg. The situation was extremely tragic, and the spread of the fire was unusually peculiar, with the fire crossing the road for more than two zhang. The details of the time will be recorded later.

Pan's Family Members:

Tangjiawan Road in Nanshi belongs to the jurisdiction of the Second District General Office of the Public Security Bureau in the Chinese territory, and the French Concession is nearby. The landlord of No. 71 is Pan A'xin (50 years old) from Zhejiang, who has been running a teahouse. Pan's wife, Zhang (35 years old), along with their two sons, A Mao (19 years old) and A Bao (4 years old), and two daughters, Xiu Ying (13 years old) and Xiao Bao (2 years old), a family of six, live in the front building of the house.

Tenants:

In addition to Pan's family living in the front building, the back building is rented to Chen Guobao (42 years old), a barber from Yangzhou, and his wife, Xu (38 years old). They have three sons and two daughters: the eldest son, Da Dong, is 17 years old, the second son, Er Dong, is 15 years old, and the third son, San Dong, is 11 years old. The fourth daughter, nicknamed Lao Hu, is 6 years old, and the fifth daughter, Xiao Long, is only 4 years old. The pavilion room is rented to Feng Zigui (42 years old), who sells fruit and runs Yang Fu Ji Woodworking.

Lack of Water for Firefighting:

At 10:15 yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the downstairs of the house due to carelessness in cooking lunch. The fire brigades from Nanshi heard the alarm and rushed to the rescue, but the water supply in the area was weak, and the water pressure was less than one zhang, making it impossible to put out the fire. Fortunately, the nearby French Concession temporarily borrowed tap water for use, but in the meantime, the fire had crossed the road. By the time it was completely extinguished at 11:00 noon, four stores had been destroyed.

Neighboring Damage:

After No. 71 was completely destroyed, the first to suffer was the clothing store at No. 69 next door. There were nine households living in the store, all workers and hawkers. Before long, the flames crossed the road for more than two zhang and spread to Xu Longxing Noodle Shop at No. 72, owned by Xu Jingou (35 years old, from Chongming), and Renji Rickshaw Company at No. 74. None of the households were insured, and the estimated loss was about 5,000 yuan.

Mrs. Xu Flees for Her Life:

It is said that the fire at No. 71 started behind the downstairs handrail, so the handrail was burned first. Most of the residents upstairs escaped through the windows or sun deck, but Chen Guobao in the back building was working in the store. Only Chen Xu and his third son, San Dong, and two young daughters, Lao Hu and Xiao Long, were at home. Mrs. Xu saw that the stairs were broken and there was no way to escape, so she urgently led San Dong to jump from the front building window.

Death and Injury:

When Mrs. Xu jumped down, her head hit the ground first, and her brains splattered. San Dong broke his leg and was taken to the hospital by ambulance. Mrs. Xu died on the way due to serious injuries. San Dong's life may be saved, but he may be disabled. It is said that Mrs. Xu was also six months pregnant. Fortunately, the two eldest sons were studying hairdressing outside, otherwise they would have suffered the same disaster.

Two Young Girls' Corpses:

When the fire was raging, it was extremely chaotic, and the number of people could not be counted. After it was completely extinguished, two girls' corpses were found in the back building, which were the two young daughters of Mrs. Xu, Lao Hu and Xiao Long. Their bodies were charred beyond recognition. The Second District General Office ordered a senior police officer to conduct a detailed investigation and first arrested the fire starter, Yang Yunlou, and then ordered the local bailiff to report to the court for inspection. Until last night, the corpses of the two children were still lying on the road, and the scene was like the completion ceremony of the National Martial Arts Hall martial arts competition.

The construction of the Central National Martial Arts Hall Competition Ground has been completed. The completion ceremony will be held at 2 pm on the 17th. The interior can accommodate more than 1,000 people. The magnificent new building will add glory to the future of national martial arts. In the past few days, dozens of people have gone to Beijing from Shanghai to participate in the ceremony. It is said that the hall has invited people from all walks of life in the party, government, military, and academia to visit. It has received many congratulatory gifts. It is said that the hall has appointed Li Zimao as the general commander of the venue, Weng Guoxun, Wang Weifan, Chen Weiping, and Nie Yurun to entertain special guests, Guo Xisan and others to entertain military and political figures, Chen Jiazhen to entertain the press, Lan Fengsan and others to entertain academics, and Li Chengbin and others to entertain other guests. Director Zhang is the chief judge, Tang Fansheng is the judge, and Zhu Guofu is the competition committee member. In addition to the ceremony, martial arts competitions will be held to live up to the name of martial arts competition. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Timing of Water Cutoff at Xinde Fang Leads to Dispute

Tenants Want Water All Day

Landlords Want to Charge Extra for Water

Authorities Decide Based on Majority

Xinde Fang on Qiujiang Road in Zhabei has 50 houses. Originally, the water fee was included in the rent. Since the installation of water meters, the landlords, in order to control water waste, stipulated that water would be supplied from 7:30 am to 12:00 pm and from 5:00 pm to 6:00 pm. Later, the tenants requested water all day because it was inconvenient to drink. The landlords issued a notice in August of this year that an additional water fee of 1.5 yuan per month per room would be charged for water all day. After one month, only eight families paid the fee, and the rest refused to do so. Therefore, the timing of the water cutoff was restored. Tenant Tang Mengwu filed a complaint with the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, requesting that the supply of water be restored all day. The bureau summoned both parties to inquire about the situation and observed that the tenants could tolerate the additional water fee, so it instructed the accounting office of the fang to consult each tenant for their opinions and then make a decision based on the majority.

Restructuring of the National Products Market

Business as Usual During the Restructuring Period

Since the Chinese National Products United Market decided to change its organization and plan, internal facilities will also be changed. The most important thing is to rearrange the shops in the market. New drawings have already been completed and are being printed. They will be announced to the public soon. The location of all obstacles and routes has been removed. However, in order to facilitate the purchase of national products by all sectors, business will continue as usual during this restructuring period. Due to changes in location, changes or mergers of businesses or rearrangements of businesses will inevitably occur for the participating manufacturers. It will be completed by the beginning of the first ten days of the month. In order to promote local products from all over the country, the market welcomes merchants from all over the country to join with special local products. Merchants from Sichuan, Anhui, Zhejiang, and other provinces have already contacted the market. The market hopes that people from all provinces in Shanghai will work hard to collect local products from their provinces and join as much as possible to facilitate sales. Therefore, a part of the future plan will be for national product factory products, and a part will be for local products from all over the country to meet the needs of society. Therefore, both foreign factories and local product merchants can contact the market to visit and learn about the methods.

Cross-Border Electricity Connection Negotiations

Chinese Constables in the Interior Have Been Withdrawn

Recently, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities dispatched workers to erect electric poles and wires on Zhongshan Road in West Shanghai. This project passed through the Hongqiao Road, which was built beyond the border. The British Municipal Council dispatched armed Chinese constables to stop the work in the Daxilu and Hongqiao Road areas. After the Sixth District, Second Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Daxilu Police Station, Officer Wang, and Hongqiao Road Officer Li, learned that the land belonged to the Chinese territory, they questioned how the police station could overstep its authority. Therefore, they led police officers to inquire with the constables. They said they were ordered to prevent the installation of Chinese merchant's electric wires passing through Daxilu, etc. Officers Wang and Li reported this to their chief. Chief Liu personally went to investigate and then went to the Jing'an Temple Police Station to seriously negotiate with the head constable, stating that Hongqiao Road and Daxilu were built beyond the border and foreigners should not interfere with any construction. It was inappropriate for the Municipal Council to dispatch constables to prevent the installation of electric wires. For the sake of diplomatic relations, the constables dispatched to both roads should be withdrawn as soon as possible to avoid misunderstandings, otherwise, I (Chief Liu referring to himself) would exercise my authority to disarm the dispatched constables, arrest them, and send them to the bureau for higher authorities to handle. After Chief Liu repeatedly negotiated and argued with the constables, they finally agreed to withdraw. Therefore, the constables dispatched to both roads were withdrawn yesterday.

Telegraphed Commander Xiong to Notify

Tragic Disaster in Taian, Shandong After the War

Report Received by the Jisheng Society

The Chinese Jisheng Society recently received reports from twenty legal entities, including the Taian Red Swastika Society, stating that Taian, Shandong, is a place with barren land and impoverished people, coupled with years of locust plagues. The households lack storage, and the population is dense. Usually, they need to buy firewood and rice to make a living. After the city was closed, the water supply was cut off first, and the fuel was immediately exhausted. The people became pale. The suffering of the food supply was already unbearable, and the attack by artillery fire was even more severe. Airplanes came from afar and bombs struck nearby. Walls collapsed and houses crumbled, blood flowed across the ground, and the dead were not cared for. Many soldiers hid in the ground to eat, and the people were exposed under thatched roofs. The number of casualties from each bombing was incalculable. When the landmine exploded, the city walls collapsed, huge rocks flew into the sky, and grease and blood soaked the ground. Feet were found among the tiles, and broken arms were found in the ditches. Crops cannot be harvested, and there is no money to buy firewood and rice. As the saying goes, there is bound to be a year of famine after a major war. Alas, we, the survivors, have suffered such a rare catastrophe since ancient times. Our souls are still in shock, and famine is imminent. The dead have no coffins, and the living lack clothing and food, no house to live in, and no place to escape. Wailing echoes in the wilderness, and dry throats eagerly await the Western River. We implore your esteemed society to show compassion and universal relief, and to provide emergency assistance. We humbly accept your kindness and await your orders. The society has previously handled disaster relief work for the Shu River project in Shandong, the relief for the Yan Yao warehouse disaster in Jinan, and now it is also transporting relief supplies to Qufu for the disaster and epidemic. The previous reports detailed the extreme suffering in Taian due to famine and war. The refugees have not yet gathered, and the aftermath needs to be planned. The tragic situation is unbearable to read, and my heart is burning with anxiety. All my compatriots are shocked by what they see. With the benevolent spirit of giving and resolving, we can alleviate the urgency of the disaster and take advantage of the opportunity to create blessings. Why not start now?

Local news from this city is transferred to the following page.

Page 15

Local News 2

Hundred Thousand Yuan Robbery Case - The Contents Are Quite Peculiar

The Thief Zhu Dexin, Escorted Back from Tianjin

Said to Be Related to Wang Jingwei's Representative

Shaved His Beard and Pulled Out His Teeth But Was Eventually Captured

Wang E and Wang Yang Are Approved to Be Transferred to Jiaxing

The case of the 100,000 yuan robbery of the Zhejiang Provincial Bank in Hangzhou has been reported in detail in the newspapers. The detectives who were dispatched to Tianjin to transfer the main suspect, Zhu Dexin (also known as Zhu Dexinsheng and Zhu Cheng), have escorted him back to Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon, along with Liang Houbiao, Sheng Cheng, Wang E, Wang Yang, Liang Dingyi, He Guo, He Xiangquan, and the women Hua Wangshi, Liang Lvshi, and He Xushi, who were arrested in Shanghai, they were all transferred to the Special District Court. Presiding Judge Zhou Hanting and Prosecutor Xu also attended the court to perform their duties. After the police lawyer Ru Bao-yi stated the facts of the case, Western Detective Wheelcox reported the circumstances of the transfer of the Zhu thief to Tianjin, as follows:

Strictly Investigate Those with Beards and Gold Teeth

After the police captured Liang Houbiao and others, Liang confessed that Zhu was the leader of the case, and that he had taken the Fengtian ship to Tianjin on August 30. He also described Zhu's appearance, stating that he had a beard and gold teeth. The police then telegraphed the Tianjin Municipal Council based on the above confession, requesting that passengers be carefully checked when the ship arrives, and that those with beards and gold teeth be strictly investigated. The Tianjin Municipal Council received the telegram and, fearing that it would be difficult to check the passengers when the ship arrived, sent an officer to meet the ship at Dagukou. After the ship arrived there, the officer boarded the ship and searched everywhere, but there were no passengers with the above-mentioned appearance.

The Beard Has Been Removed and the Teeth Have Been Pulled Out

Just as they were hesitating, another passenger named Xiong Jiandong reported to the searchers that he had seen a passenger shave his beard and pull out his gold teeth the night before. He led the searchers to the engine room and arrested the person who had shaved his beard and pulled out his teeth. After questioning, they learned that he was Zhu Dexin.

Xiong Jiandong Is Actually Li Zuquan

The Zhu thief tried to bribe a searcher surnamed Chen with cash, hoping to be released, and was willing to pay an additional 600 yuan after arriving in Tianjin. The searcher refused. When the ship arrived in Tianjin, Zhu, Xiong Jiandong, and their luggage were taken to the Tianjin Municipal Council's police station. Zhu initially denied being a thief and said that he did not know Xiong. After the Tianjin police checked Xiong's luggage, they did not find any contraband, so they released Xiong. The next day, the Zhu thief suddenly claimed that the person released yesterday was not Xiong Jiandong, but his gang leader, Li Zuquan.
